## O61 — Declare the 'Danvers Statement' as a Biblically Faithful Declaration
**Targets:** (statement — non-provision) · **Source:** Calvary · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/Overture-61_Calvary_Danvers.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/Overture-61_Calvary_Danvers.pdf)

**What it does:** Asks GA53 to declare the Council on Biblical Manhood & Womanhood's "Danvers Statement on Biblical Manhood and Womanhood" a biblically faithful declaration, and to refer it to the Committee on Discipleship Ministries (CDM) for inclusion and promotion among denominational teaching materials. It seeks to establish complementarianism as a "first principle" of the PCA, expressly modeled on the 2019 Nashville Statement declaration (a "declaration," not a constitutional "adoption").

**Cites in its own grounds:** GA47 O4 (2019) — the PCA's declaration of the Nashville Statement as biblically faithful (cited as the controlling template); and the 2009 decline of an overture to adopt the Danvers Statement (GA37 O13), which it acknowledges ("an overture to adopt it was declined by the General Assembly in 2009") and distinguishes by reframing its ask as a non-constitutional declaration.

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
None found.

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
None found.

### Prior overtures
- **[GA37 O13](../overtures/ga37_2009__o13.md)** (2009, Answered in the negative) — "Adopt the Danvers Statement on Gender Issues" (Presbytery of Grace). The exact prior attempt at the same change; O61 itself cites it as the 2009 decline and reframes its ask as a "declaration" rather than an "adoption" to avoid that outcome. [page](../markdown/ga37_2009.md#ga37-p279), [debate](../markdown/ga37_2009.md#ga37-p308), [index](../markdown/ga37_2009.md#ga37-p588)
- **[GA47 O4](../overtures/ga47_2019__o4.md)** (2019, Adopted final) — "Declare the Nashville Statement on Biblical Sexuality a Biblically Faithful Declaration" (Calvary Presbytery — same presbytery). The direct precedent and explicit template; O61 is the companion gender-roles statement to the 2019 sexuality statement. [page](../markdown/ga47_2019.md#ga47-p589), [debate](../markdown/ga47_2019.md#ga47-p645), [index](../markdown/ga47_2019.md#ga47-p761)
- **[GA47 O22](../overtures/ga47_2019__o22.md)** (2019, Answered by reference) — "Urge Assembly to Adopt Overture 4 Endorsing the Nashville Statement" (Philadelphia Metro West). Shows how the assembly handled a companion/supporting overture to a "biblically faithful" declaration; bears on the procedural fate of O61-style supporting actions. [page](../markdown/ga47_2019.md#ga47-p645), [index](../markdown/ga47_2019.md#ga47-p762)
- **[GA48 O38](../overtures/ga48_2021__o38.md)** (2021, Adopted final) — "Commend the Ad Interim Committee's Human Sexuality Report" (Calvary Presbytery, to OC, CDM). ⭐ Same presbytery and the same CDM-referral mechanism O61 invokes (commend/refer a theological document to CDM for teaching use rather than constitutionalize it). [page](../markdown/ga48_2021.md#ga48-p1073), [debate](../markdown/ga48_2021.md#ga48-p1131)

### RPR exceptions
None found.

### Note
The deterministic join returned no provisions (a theological declaration, not a BCO amendment), so cases/inquiries/RPR are empty from the spine; the entries above come from a topical search of /workspace/index (OVERTURES.md, overture_bodies.jsonl, cases.jsonl, INQUIRIES.md, CCB-OVERTURE-ADVICE.md) on "Danvers / Nashville / manhood / womanhood / complementarian / human sexuality." PRUNED as incidental: the human-sexuality CCB advice items (GA49 CI07 on BCO 16-4; GA50 CI06 on BCO 7; GA50 CI17 on BCO 8-3) construe proposed *constitutional* amendments, not a statement declaration. Also PRUNED: SJC/CJB cases touching complementarian doctrine in *ordination/examination* disputes (the John Wood Matter 2001, Bogue v. Ascension 1987, Urish v. Rocky Mountain 2010 on 1 Tim 2:12, Reese & Bech v. Philadelphia 2014 on women deacons) — these adjudicate specific officer-qualification facts and do not construe the Danvers/Nashville Statements or the GA's power to declare a statement biblically faithful, the actual question O61 raises. The genuinely bearing line is the overture history: the 2009 Danvers decline (GA37 O13) and the 2019 Nashville declaration (GA47 O4 / O22), with GA48 O38 as the closest recent example of Calvary referring a theological document to CDM. Also note the broader sexuality-statement-to-polity pipeline (GA49 O33–35 commending the Human Sexuality Report; GA50 O9/O24 amending BCO 7 and 8-3) as background context, though those are amendment overtures rather than declaration overtures and so do not bear directly.

## O62 — Divide Tennessee Valley Presbytery into Two Presbyteries
**Targets:** (boundaries) · **Source:** TVP · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/03/Overture-62_TVP_Dividing.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/03/Overture-62_TVP_Dividing.pdf)

**What it does:** Asks GA53 to divide Tennessee Valley Presbytery (36 churches, 5 missions, 113 ministers, 32 counties) into a continuing TVP (13 southern counties: 8 in TN + 5 in GA, ~24 churches) and a new Smoky Mountain Presbytery (19 northern TN counties around Knoxville, ~12 churches + 4 missions), effective January 1, 2027, with rules for assigning RUF / Covenant College / MTW / MNA / HR / out-of-bounds teaching elders and candidates.

**Cites in its own grounds:** The "Guidelines for Dividing Presbyteries" membership thresholds ("minimum of 10 churches," "total communicant membership of at least 1,000," "at least 3 churches having a membership of at least 125"), which O62 attributes to the 41st GA (see Note — these were in fact adopted by the 26th GA). No prior cases, overtures, or inquiries cited by name.

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
None found.

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
- **CI 10-77** (GA10/1982, advice given) — Constitutionality of a non-geographical presbytery: the CCB found BCO 11-4 "implies geographical bounds" while BCO 13-1 does not limit "bounds" geographically. Bears on the constitutional premise of any geographic-boundary division like O62, which redraws bounds county-by-county. [page](../inquiries/ga10_1982__ci04.md)

### Prior overtures
- **[GA22 O27](../overtures/ga22_1994__o27.md)** (1994, Adopted (final)) — "Divide Tennessee Valley Presbytery to Form Nashville Presbytery." The single most on-point precedent: the prior division of *this very presbytery*, confirming GA's established practice of granting TVP's subdivision requests. [page](../markdown/ga22_1994.md#ga22-p65)
- **[GA41 O9](../overtures/ga41_2013__o9.md)** (2013, Adopted (final)) — "Form Tidewater Presbytery from James River Presbytery." The structural template O62 follows almost verbatim — same Guidelines criteria (≥10 churches / ≥1,000 communicants / ≥3 churches of ≥125), same Jan 1 effective date — and it correctly attributes those Guidelines to the *26th* GA. [page](../markdown/ga41_2013.md#ga41-p91)
- **[GA45 O19](../overtures/ga45_2017__o19.md)** (2017, Adopted (final)) — "Divide the Presbytery of the Southwest into Two Presbyteries." Recent precedent for granting a presbytery's request to split into two. [page](../markdown/ga45_2017.md#ga45-p673)
- **GA46 O22 / O23** (2018, Adopted (final)) — "Divide Metropolitan New York Presbytery into Two Presbyteries." Recent two-way division granted; O23 was the companion sent to CCB/OC for editorial review. [page](../markdown/ga46_2018.md#ga46-p715) · [O23 page](../markdown/ga46_2018.md#ga46-p717)
- **GA52 O36 / O46** (2025, O36 Adopted (final)) — "Change the Boundaries of Georgia Foothills and Metro Atlanta Presbyteries." ⭐ Most recent boundary action; shows GA53-era MNA practice of approving paired boundary overtures. [page](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p1273) · [O46 page](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p1297)

### RPR exceptions
None found.

### Note
This is a non-provision (boundaries) overture, so the deterministic provision-join spine returned no hits; all bearing actions above were found by topical search of the OVERTURES / INQUIRIES indices. **Provenance caveat on O62's own grounds:** O62 attributes the "Guidelines for Dividing Presbyteries" to "the 41st General Assembly," but the Guidelines were in fact *approved by the 26th GA* (M26GA, 26-44, p.180; see [ga26_1998.md#ga26-p180](../markdown/ga26_1998.md#ga26-p180)), building on guidelines first set by the 16th GA (1988); the GA41 Tidewater overture (O9) cited them correctly as the 26th GA's and merely applied them. **Pruning:** the OVERTURES index lists dozens of routine boundary-adjustment/erection overtures (e.g., GA48 O8/O11/O42, GA49 O10, GA50 O1, GA51 O5/O8/O11/O12, GA52 O2/O17/O45); these are administrative county-shuffles, not subdivisions of an existing presbytery, so they are pruned as not bearing on the *division* question. Kept items are limited to (a) the prior division of TVP itself, (b) the closest structural template (GA41 Tidewater), and (c) recent two-way divisions plus the most recent GA52 boundary precedent for current practice. No judicial cases or RPR exceptions exist because presbytery boundaries are administrative matters handled by MNA, not justiciable provisions. (The prior pass cited GA40 O38, GA14 O9/O15, GA35 O17, GA36 O10, and "companion" overtures O10/O44/O70/O87 — none verified against the corpus and given without deep-links; they are dropped here.)

## O63 — Amend RAO 19-4 to Establish Preference in Recognition for an Objector to an In Gross Motion
**Targets:** RAO 19-4 · **Source:** South Texas · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/03/Overture-63_SouthTexas_RAO19-4.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/03/Overture-63_SouthTexas_RAO19-4.pdf)

**What it does:** Adds a new RAO 19-4.f providing that, when a commissioner objects to including an in gross recommendation or overture (under RAO 14-9.d or 15-8.b) and it is pulled for separate debate, the objecting commissioner "shall have preference in recognition (see RONR [12th ed.] 42:7) when debating the separated recommendation" — i.e., recognized first to speak on the item he pulled out.

**Cites in its own grounds:** None. Cites only the provisions it edits/cross-references (RAO 14-9.d, 15-8.b, RAO 19) and the parliamentary authority (RONR [12th ed.] 42, 42:7, 42:9.1). No prior PCA cases, overtures, or inquiries are cited.

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
None found.

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
None found.

### Prior overtures
- **[GA37 O2](../overtures/ga37_2009__o2.md)** (2009, Adopted (final)) — "Amend RAO 19-4.d, 14-9.h, and 15-8.g Governing Debate on Minority Reports" (Potomac, to CCB/OC). The only prior overture to amend the very same provision, RAO 19-4; directly construes the omnibus/separated-debate recognition machinery O63 now edits. [page](../markdown/ga37_2009.md#ga37-p57), [p.309](../markdown/ga37_2009.md#ga37-p307), [p.589](../markdown/ga37_2009.md#ga37-p587)
- **[GA50 O3](../overtures/ga50_2023__o3.md)** (2023) — "Amend RAO 14-9.h and 15-8.g to Limit General Assembly Debate" (James River, to CCB/OC). ⭐ Touches the same in gross / separated-debate provisions (RAO 14-9, 15-8) O63 cross-references; a recent companion attempt to regulate floor debate on pulled items. [page](../markdown/ga50_2023.md#ga50-p969), [p.1083](../markdown/ga50_2023.md#ga50-p1075)
- **[GA50 O22](../overtures/ga50_2023__o22.md)** (2023, Answered in the negative) — "Amend RAO 8-4.h, 17-1, and 19-2 to Specify When Minority Reports Are Permitted" (Session of First Presbyterian Church, to CCB/OC/SJC). ⭐ A recent failed attempt to amend RAO 19 (chapter 19-2) governing floor procedure; bears on the Assembly's recent appetite for fine-tuning RAO 19 debate rules. [page](../markdown/ga50_2023.md#ga50-p1019), [p.1085](../markdown/ga50_2023.md#ga50-p1077)

### RPR exceptions
None found.

### Note
Pruned: the spine returned nine RPR rows for **BCO** 19-4 (e.g. [South Texas, 32nd/2004](../rpr/south-texas.md); [Northwest Georgia, 41st/2013](../rpr/northwest-georgia.md)) — all concern the Book of Church Order's licensure-form/recording requirement, an entirely different document from the **RAO** (Rules of Assembly Operations) that O63 amends. They are incidental and excluded. The only provision-exact bearing action is GA37 O2 (amended RAO 19-4.d); GA50 O3 and O22 are topical supplements for the closely-related RAO 14-9 / 15-8 / 19-2 debate provisions O63 cross-references. No renumbering applies (RAO is not in the BCO renumbering map). No judicial case or constitutional inquiry/CCB-advice item construes RAO 19-4 (a prior draft's citation of a "GA50 II.O / ci15" CCB advice on RAO 19-2 was checked against CCB-OVERTURE-ADVICE.md and the corpus join and could not be substantiated, so it was removed). O63 is referred to CCB + OC, so CCB constitutional review at GA53 is expected.

## O64 — Amend BCO 23-2 to Establish Associate Membership for Honorably Retired TEs
**Targets:** BCO 23-2 · **Source:** Canada West · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/03/Overture-64_CanadaWest_23-2.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/03/Overture-64_CanadaWest_23-2.pdf)

**What it does:** Amends BCO 23-2 so that a medically-disabled or honorably-retired TE retaining membership in his Presbytery must also maintain an active associate membership (or equivalent) in a faithful local church, subject to the same limitations as BCO 46-4 — securing local pastoral care, oversight, and accountability for retired ministers.

**Cites in its own grounds:** None (cites only BCO 23-2 itself and BCO 46-4 as the "paradigm and precedent for associate membership"; no prior cases, overtures, or inquiries are named).

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
None found. *(The provision-exact spine returned [Bigelow v. North Florida Presbytery (2024-5)](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p983), but it cites BCO 23-2 incidentally among ~40 provisions in a discipline/jurisdiction appeal and does not construe the membership/oversight question O64 raises — pruned. See Note.)*

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
- **17-82 III,19** (GA17/1989, not in conflict) — Illiana Presbytery's standing rule relieving retired ministers from mandatory reporting was found not in conflict with BCO 23-2, with the presbytery advised to use its own wisdom under BCO 41-5. Bears directly: speaks to the very gap O64 targets — that retired TEs receive less active oversight/accountability under 23-2. [page](../inquiries/ga17_1989__ci04.md)
- **31-56 VI** (GA31/2003, in conflict) — Overture restricting presbytery/GA voting to pastors only held in conflict with BCO 3-1 and 14-2; 23-2 cited as part of the set defining TE membership rights. Bears on the "rights and privileges" of retired-TE presbytery membership that O64 leaves intact. [page](../inquiries/ga31_2003__ci09.md)
- **32-40 II.D** (GA32/2004, in conflict) — CCB reaffirmed (re-raising the same proposal) that restricting voting to pastors disenfranchises non-pastor TEs; same 23-2 membership-rights cluster. [page](../inquiries/ga32_2004__ci04.md)

### Prior overtures
- **[GA52 O25](../overtures/ga52_2025__o25.md)** (2025, no recorded outcome) — Northwest Georgia Presbytery, "Amend BCO 46-4 to Add Associate Membership Class for Honorably Retired TEs." ⭐ Direct companion/precursor: the immediately-prior attempt at the *same* reform (associate membership for retired TEs), routed through 46-4 rather than 23-2 as O64 does. [page](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p1238)
- **[GA26 O1](../overtures/ga26_1998__o1.md)** (1999, Approved & ratified) — Potomac Presbytery, "Amend BCO 13-5 to Clarify Membership of One Honorably Retired." Prior, *successful* clarification of the membership status of an honorably-retired minister — the same membership question O64 reopens for 23-2. [page](../markdown/ga26_1998.md#ga26-p49)
- **[GA32 O8](../overtures/ga32_2004__o8.md)** (2005, Approved & ratified) — North Texas Presbytery, "Amend BCO 24-9 to Delete Age Requirement for Ruling Elder and Deacon Emeritus Status." Adjacent: alters honored-officer (emeritus) status, but for RE/deacons under 24-9, not retired-TE membership/oversight; weaker bearing. [page](../markdown/ga32_2004.md#ga32-p163)

### RPR exceptions
- **BCO 23-2** — 3 citations show real-world friction at exactly O64's seam: [Eastern Pennsylvania](../rpr/exc/eastern-pennsylvania__015.md) (48th/2021) — a TE cannot simultaneously be honorably retired and an Associate Pastor; and [Missouri](../rpr/exc/missouri__055.md) (50th/2023 raised, 51st/2024 satisfactory) — an honorably-retired minister released to the care of a church session (i.e., presbyteries already experimenting with local-church homes for retired TEs). [by provision](../index/RPR-BY-PROVISION.md)

### Note
**Companion cross-link:** O64 is the 23-2 counterpart to **[GA52 O25](../overtures/ga52_2025__o25.md)** (which sought the same associate-membership-for-retired-TEs result via 46-4); read together. **Pruning:** the provision-exact spine's lone judicial hit (Bigelow 2024-5) cites 23-2 only in passing within a large discipline/jurisdiction appeal and does not bear — pruned from the cases section. The voting-restriction inquiries (31-56, 32-40) cite 23-2 within the TE membership-rights cluster rather than the retirement/oversight question, so they bear only obliquely; 17-82 (retired-minister oversight) is the on-point inquiry. **No renumbering** affects BCO 23-2 (no entry in bco_renumberings.jsonl for chapter 23). The RPR row from Missouri (retired TE released to a session's care) is the strongest evidence of live presbytery practice anticipating O64's local-church-membership requirement.

---

## O65 — Amend BCO 38-1 re Confessions and Cases without Process
**Targets:** BCO 38-1 · **Source:** Canada West · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/03/Overture-65_CanadaWest_38-1.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/03/Overture-65_CanadaWest_38-1.pdf)

**What it does:** Rewrites BCO 38-1 to require, in a case without process, an approved, co-signed written "Confession" (sufficient summary of facts, specific confession, and evidence of repentance) appended to the minutes; bars any other information without written consent of accused and court (incl. prosecutors, committees, commissions); guarantees the right to appeal (BCO 42) and to counsel (BCO 32-19); codifies a procedure for informing and inviting comment from offended parties (BCO 29-3); and adds a track for when someone other than the offender reveals the offense (court investigates and may draw up a confession document the accused may sign, else proceed with process).

**Cites in its own grounds:** None (the rationale cites no specific cases, overtures, or inquiries — only cross-references BCO 42, 32-19, and 29-3).

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
- **[2008-17 — Hutchinson & Bulkeley v. Western Carolina](../cases/ga38_2010__2008-15_2008-16_2008-17_2008-18_2009-01_2009-03.md)** (GA38/2010, not_sustained) — Squarely a BCO 38-1 case-without-process complaint over the censure imposed; construes the limits of judgment-without-process. [minutes](../markdown/ga38_2010.md#ga38-p177)
- **[2008-18 — Hutchinson & Bulkeley v. Western Carolina](../cases/ga38_2010__2008-15_2008-16_2008-17_2008-18_2009-01_2009-03.md)** (GA38/2010, not_sustained) — Companion no-process case on a commission's opinion; part of the factual matrix the later jurisprudence treats as the leading 38-1 "confession" precedent. [minutes](../markdown/ga38_2010.md#ga38-p180)
- **[2008-16 — Hutchinson & Bulkeley v. Western Carolina](../cases/ga38_2010__2008-15_2008-16_2008-17_2008-18_2009-01_2009-03.md)** (GA45/2017 citation) — Cited as precedent: a presbytery commission, having found a strong presumption of guilt, assisted the accused in preparing a confession — exactly the "court draws up / approves a confession document" mechanic O65 codifies. [minutes](../markdown/ga45_2017.md#ga45-p539)
- **[2009-10 — Woodward v. Western Carolina Presbytery](../cases/ga38_2010__2009-05_2009-08_2009-09_2009-10.md)** (GA38/2010, sustained_in_part) — No-process discipline reviewed under 38-1; bears on what the record must show. [minutes](../markdown/ga38_2010.md#ga38-p197)
- **[2009-21 — Armes v. Southwest Florida Presbytery](../cases/ga39_2011__2009-12_2009-21.md)** (GA39/2011, sustained) — Sustained complaint over the adequacy of a case-without-process record under 38-1. [minutes](../markdown/ga39_2011.md#ga39-p532)
- **[2009-22 — McNeil v. Chesapeake Presbytery](../cases/ga39_2011__2009-22.md)** (GA39/2011, denied) — 38-1 confession/judgment-without-process challenge. [minutes](../markdown/ga39_2011.md#ga39-p537)
- **[2011-17 — Smith v. Mississippi Valley Presbytery](../cases/ga41_2013__2011-17.md)** (GA41/2013, sustained) — Sustained on a 38-1 deficiency; the recurring "no full statement / improper confession record" friction O65 targets. [minutes](../markdown/ga41_2013.md#ga41-p557)
- **[2011-18 — Ruff v. Nashville Presbytery](../cases/ga41_2013__2011-18.md)** (GA41/2013, sustained) — Sustained 38-1 complaint over an improperly handled case without process. [minutes](../markdown/ga41_2013.md#ga41-p568)
- **[2015-11 — Thompson v. South Florida Presbytery](../cases/ga44_2016__2015-11.md)** (GA44/2016, sustained) — Sustained complaint construing 38-1 confession/no-process requirements. [minutes](../markdown/ga44_2016.md#ga44-p541)
- **[2016-15 — Bachmann v. Nashville Presbytery](../cases/ga46_2018__2016-15.md)** (GA46/2018, sustained) — Sustained 38-1 case-without-process complaint. [minutes](../markdown/ga46_2018.md#ga46-p528)
- **[2019-10 — Evans and Pitts et al. v. Arizona Presbytery](../cases/ga48_2021__2019-10_2019-12.md)** (GA48/2021, sustained) — ⭐ Recent sustained 38-1 case; prominent no-process discipline failure. [minutes](../markdown/ga48_2021.md#ga48-p788)
- **[2019-12 — Pitts et al. v. Arizona Presbytery](../cases/ga48_2021__2019-10_2019-12.md)** (GA48/2021, sustained) — ⭐ Companion sustained 38-1 case. [minutes](../markdown/ga48_2021.md#ga48-p788)
- **[2019-11 — Crouse v. Northwest Georgia Presbytery](../cases/ga48_2021__2019-11.md)** (GA48/2021, denied) — ⭐ 38-1 no-process challenge. [minutes](../markdown/ga48_2021.md#ga48-p804)
- **[2021-10 — Williams v. Chesapeake Presbytery](../cases/ga49_2022__2021-10.md)** (GA49/2022, denied) — ⭐ 38-1 confession-handling dispute. [minutes](../markdown/ga49_2022.md#ga49-p902)
- **[2021-11 — Park et al. v. Korean Central Presbytery](../cases/ga50_2023__2021-11.md)** (GA50/2023, sustained) — ⭐ Sustained 38-1 case-without-process complaint. [minutes](../markdown/ga50_2023.md#ga50-p805)
- **[2022-23 — Woodham v. South Florida Presbytery](../cases/ga51_2024__2022-23.md)** (GA51/2024, denied) — ⭐ 38-1 confession/no-process matter. [minutes](../markdown/ga51_2024.md#ga51-p749)
- **[2023-19 — Huffman v. Tennessee Valley Presbytery](../cases/ga51_2024__2023-19.md)** (GA51/2024, other) — ⭐ 38-1 case-without-process matter. [minutes](../markdown/ga51_2024.md#ga51-p959)
- **[2023-12 — Flatgard v. Metro Atlanta Presbytery](../cases/ga52_2025__2023-12.md)** (GA52/2025, sustained) — ⭐ Most recent sustained 38-1 case; continuing real-world friction with no-process records. [minutes](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p820)
- **[2023-18 — Sears v. Nashville Presbytery](../cases/ga52_2025__2023-18.md)** (GA52/2025, denied) — ⭐ Recent 38-1 confession-handling matter. [minutes](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p867)
- **[2024-18 — Harris v. Wisconsin Presbytery](../cases/ga52_2025__2024-18.md)** (GA52/2025, denied) — ⭐ Recent 38-1 case-without-process matter. [minutes](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p1037)

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
- **II.W** (GA48/2021) — Confession-document requirements for cases without process; CCB found amending 38-1 to require confession documentation not in conflict — directly the written-Confession requirement O65 codifies. [page](../inquiries/ga48_2021__ci23.md)
- **II.X** (GA48/2021) — Confession-timing requirements in cases without process (38-1, 42-2); not in conflict, adopted. [page](../inquiries/ga48_2021__ci24.md)
- **II.Y** (GA48/2021) — Right to counsel in discipline cases without process; not in conflict — O65's counsel guarantee (BCO 32-19) tracks this. [page](../inquiries/ga48_2021__ci25.md)
- **II.L** (GA48/2021) — Appealing a censure imposed without formal process (38-1, 42-2); not in conflict — O65's "right to appeal (BCO 42)" clause. [page](../inquiries/ga48_2021__ci12.md)
- **II.T** (GA50/2023) — Confessions and rights of offended parties in 38-1; not in conflict — directly the offended-party comment/notice process O65 adds. [page](../inquiries/ga50_2023__ci20.md)
- **II.J** (GA52/2025) — Court's permissible interactions with an offended party under 38-1; not in conflict — ⭐ most recent CCB advice on the offended-party mechanic O65 restates. [page](../inquiries/ga52_2025__ci10.md)
- **Supplemental II.A** (GA49/2022) — Seven 48th-GA overtures (incl. 19/33/34/35 on 38-1) held over; CCB found all not in conflict. [page](../inquiries/ga49_2022__ci27.md)

### Prior overtures
- **[GA27 O11](../overtures/ga27_1999__o11.md)** (1999, Approved & ratified 2000) — "Amend BCO 38-1 to Clarify Confession of Guilt Procedure" (Pittsburgh) — the original clarification of the confession-of-guilt procedure O65 now rebuilds. [page](../markdown/ga27_1999.md#ga27-p164)
- **[GA44 O39](../overtures/ga44_2016__o39.md)** (2016, Answered in the negative) — "Amend BCO 38-1 and 42-2 to Allow Appeal in Cases Without Process" (Pacific NW) — first failed attempt at the appeal-right O65 includes. [page](../markdown/ga44_2016.md#ga44-p639)
- **[GA44 O53](../overtures/ga44_2016__o53.md)** (2016, Answered by reference) — "Encourage Individual Repentance for Racial Sin via BCO 38-1" (NW Georgia) — uses the 38-1 confession mechanism. [page](../markdown/ga44_2016.md#ga44-p664)
- **[GA48 O19](../overtures/ga48_2021__o19.md)** (2021) — "Amend BCO 38-1 and 42-2 to Allow Appeal of Censure in a Case Without Process" (Pacific NW, Revised) — ⭐ the appeal-right amendment (CCB II.L). [page](../markdown/ga48_2021.md#ga48-p991)
- **[GA48 O33](../overtures/ga48_2021__o33.md)** (2021) — "Amend BCO 38-1 to Require Written Confession Document in Cases Without Process" (Pacific NW) — ⭐ the written-Confession requirement central to O65 (CCB II.W). [page](../markdown/ga48_2021.md#ga48-p1062)
- **[GA48 O34](../overtures/ga48_2021__o34.md)** (2021) — "Amend BCO 38-1 to Clarify Confession Timing in Cases Without Process" (Pacific NW) — ⭐ confession-timing amendment (CCB II.X). [page](../markdown/ga48_2021.md#ga48-p1063)
- **[GA48 O35](../overtures/ga48_2021__o35.md)** (2021) — "Amend BCO 38-1 to Guarantee Right to Counsel in Cases Without Process" (Pacific NW) — ⭐ the counsel guarantee O65 carries (CCB II.Y). [page](../markdown/ga48_2021.md#ga48-p1064)
- **[GA50 O27](../overtures/ga50_2023__o27.md)** (2023) — "Amend BCO 38-1 Regarding Confessions and Offended Parties" (Pacific NW) — ⭐ the offended-party process O65 restates (CCB II.T). [page](../markdown/ga50_2023.md#ga50-p1029)
- **[GA52 O14](../overtures/ga52_2025__o14.md)** (2025, Answered in the negative) — "Amend BCO 38-1 to Specify How a Court May Interact with an Offended Party" (Great Lakes) — ⭐ the immediately prior, recently-failed attempt at the offended-party mechanic O65 re-proposes (CCB II.J). [page](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p1195)

### RPR exceptions
- **BCO 38-1** — 21 RPR citations, recurring across presbyteries and years for failing to record the case-without-process steps — e.g. [Calvary](../rpr/exc/calvary__092.md) 42nd/2014 (TE indefinitely suspended with no record of process), [Arizona](../rpr/exc/arizona__025.md) 49th/2022 (full 38-1 statement not recorded in minutes), [Northern Illinois](../rpr/exc/northern-illinois__060.md) 51st/2024 (record of case without process not in minutes), and [Fellowship](../rpr/exc/fellowship__030.md) 52nd/2025 (court failed to invite an offended party to comment on the Confession). This is the live real-world friction O65 directly addresses: missing written confessions and missing offended-party process. [by provision](../index/RPR-BY-PROVISION.md)

### Note
O65 is essentially a consolidated re-proposal of the Pacific Northwest 38-1 reform series (GA48 O19/O33/O34/O35, GA50 O27) plus the offended-party mechanic that Great Lakes O14 failed to carry at GA52 — all of which the CCB repeatedly found "not in conflict," yet which were not fully ratified into the text. The 21 RPR exceptions and the steady stream of sustained SJC complaints (2011-17, 2011-18, 2016-15, 2019-10/12, 2021-11, 2023-12) evidence genuine, continuing friction over inadequate no-process records. PRUNING: the high-recall spine returned ~43 cases citing 38-1; I dropped roughly two dozen that merely cite 38-1 in passing or as part of a larger censure dispute without construing the confession / no-process / offended-party questions O65 changes — including the bare GA15 administrative reports (p340, p342), the unnumbered GA26/GA36 SJC entries, Chastain/Heritage 2006-7 (out of order on jurisdiction), Morton Smith 2009-2, Sherfey 2011-8, Sawyers 2011-6, Thompson 2015-10, Fordice 2016-9, Malone 2007-2 (cited only in a GA48 minute), Williams 2019-4, PCA v. MS Valley 2019-6, McWilliams 2020-3, Marusich 2020-4, the GA49 Pacific Presbytery cluster (2020-7/8/9 and Ozbalt & Barr), and the GA51 BCO 40-5 Metro NY matter. No constitutional inquiries returned (CCB advice only). No renumbering caveat: BCO 38-1 has retained its number throughout PCA history. The unrelated GA49 O26 (Statement on Political Violence) is a false body+title match and was excluded.

## O66 — Issue a Declaration of Thanksgiving on the Occasion of the 250th Anniversary of the Nation's Founding
**Targets:** (statement — invokes GA power under BCO 14-6.k) · **Source:** Philadelphia · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/03/Overture-66_Philadelphia_Thanksgiving.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/03/Overture-66_Philadelphia_Thanksgiving.pdf)

**What it does:** Asks the 53rd GA to issue a formal "Declaration of Thanksgiving for the United States of America on the Occasion of the 250th Anniversary of the Nation's Founding" on July 4, 2026 — spreading the whereas statements upon the minutes and publishing them electronically through the Administrative Committee via byFaith — and to stir the denomination to fervent prayer per WLC 191. It grounds the GA's authority in BCO 14-6.k (power "to recommend measures for the promotion of charity, truth and holiness through all the churches under its care").

**Cites in its own grounds:** No prior GA actions, cases, overtures, or inquiries. The grounds rest on Scripture, WCF 5.7/20.2/23.1, WLC 191, the Westminster Directory for Public Worship, the 1775 pastoral letter of the Synod of New York and Philadelphia, John Witherspoon's 1776 sermon, Francis Makemie's 1706 first American presbytery, and BCO 14-6.k.

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
None found.

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
None found. (The spine is provision-empty; a topical sweep of BCO 14-6 inquiries returned only matters on a different sub-question of the chapter — committee-of-commissioners authority and dissociation procedure, e.g. [ga10_1982 CI](../inquiries/ga10_1982__ci01.md) and [ga50_2023 CI](../inquiries/ga50_2023__ci21.md) — none construing the 14-6.k "recommend measures for charity, truth and holiness" power O66 invokes. Pruned as incidental; see Note.)

### Prior overtures
- **[GA3 O20](../overtures/ga03_1975__o20.md)** (1975, Adopted (final)) — "Call for a Day of Prayer and Fasting on July 4, 1976" (Grace); the PCA's own Bicentennial precedent — a July-4 national-anniversary observance — the closest direct analogue to O66's July-4 / 250th-anniversary act, 50 years prior. [p.32](../markdown/ga03_1975.md#ga03-p32)
- **[GA19 O41](../overtures/ga19_1991__o41.md)** (1991, Adopted (final)) — "Call a Day of Thanksgiving for War Victory" (Heritage); precedent for the GA issuing a corporate thanksgiving on a national occasion. [p.61](../markdown/ga19_1991.md#ga19-p59), [p.174](../markdown/ga19_1991.md#ga19-p172)
- **[GA21 O16](../overtures/ga21_1993__o16.md)** (1993, Adopted (final)) — "Issue Declaration of Conscience on Homosexuality to the President" (Potomac); precedent for the GA issuing a formal declaration touching the civil sphere. [p.56](../markdown/ga21_1993.md#ga21-p54), [p.131](../markdown/ga21_1993.md#ga21-p129)
- **[GA35 O6](../overtures/ga35_2007__o6.md)** (2007, Adopted (final)) — "Commemorate 500th Anniversary of Calvin's Birth" (Philadelphia Metro West); an anniversary-commemoration overture, bearing on the GA's practice of marking historic anniversaries. [p.578](../markdown/ga35_2007.md#ga35-p576)
- **[GA37 O18](../overtures/ga37_2009__o18.md)** (2009, Answered in the negative) — "Issue a Declaration Opposing Homosexuals Serving in the Military" (Eastern Pennsylvania); a declaration overture the GA declined — evidence the Assembly does not reflexively adopt declarations. [p.285](../markdown/ga37_2009.md#ga37-p283), [p.590](../markdown/ga37_2009.md#ga37-p588)
- **[GA40 O10](../overtures/ga40_2012__o10.md)** (2012, Answered by reference) — "Adopt Declaration Rejecting All Evolutionary Views of Adam's Origin" (Rocky Mountain); a declaration overture answered by reference rather than adopted. [p.89](../markdown/ga40_2012.md#ga40-p87), [p.796](../markdown/ga40_2012.md#ga40-p794)
- **GA40 O37 / O44** (2012, Answered by reference / Adopted (final)) — "Recognize 30th Anniversary of Church Unity (Joining & Receiving)" (Pittsburgh / New Jersey); anniversary-recognition precedent. [O37 p.743](../markdown/ga40_2012.md#ga40-p741), [O44 p.751](../markdown/ga40_2012.md#ga40-p749)
- **[GA44 O32](../overtures/ga44_2016__o32.md)** (2016, Referred) — "Call Member Churches to a Day of Prayer and Fasting" (James River); recent precedent for a denomination-wide prayer call, the worship-and-prayer dimension of O66. [p.634](../markdown/ga44_2016.md#ga44-p632), [p.743](../markdown/ga44_2016.md#ga44-p741)
- **[GA46 O35](../overtures/ga46_2018__o35.md)** (2018, Adopted (final)) — "Establish Subcommittee of AC to Plan PCA 50th Anniversary Celebration" (Southeast Alabama); recent anniversary-commemoration precedent processed through the AC, parallel to O66's AC/byFaith publication mechanism. [p.79](../markdown/ga46_2018.md#ga46-p77), [p.739](../markdown/ga46_2018.md#ga46-p737)
- **[GA47 O4](../overtures/ga47_2019__o4.md)** (2019, Adopted (final)) — "Declare the Nashville Statement on Biblical Sexuality a Biblically Faithful Declaration" (Calvary); the most recent example of the GA adopting and spreading a formal declaration upon the minutes — the closest procedural template for O66. [p.591](../markdown/ga47_2019.md#ga47-p589), [p.763](../markdown/ga47_2019.md#ga47-p761)

### RPR exceptions
None found. (O66 amends no constitutional text, so no Records-of-Presbytery exception thread is implicated.)

### Note
Non-provision overture: the deterministic spine returned `provisions=[]`, so every action above comes from a topical sweep of /workspace/index (OVERTURES.md, INQUIRIES.md, CCB-OVERTURE-ADVICE.md, CASES.md) on the three concepts O66 actually engages — (1) a national-anniversary observance, (2) a GA-issued corporate thanksgiving / day of prayer, and (3) a formal declaration spread upon the minutes. **Companion GA53 overtures** (verified via the join, to be cross-linked): **O76** (Calvary) and **O89** (Fellowship) are near-identical "Issue a Declaration of Thanksgiving for the USA on the 250th Anniversary" overtures — GA will likely consolidate O66/O76/O89 — and **O50** (MS Valley, "Call for a Day of Fasting and Prayer for Revival and Renewal of the Church") and **O4** (PNW, "Docket a Prayer of Thanksgiving for Adult Professions of Faith") are companions in the prayer/thanksgiving vein. Strongest analogues: **[GA3 O20](../overtures/ga03_1975__o20.md)** (the 1976 Bicentennial July-4 day of prayer/fasting — a 250th-vs-200th parallel) and **[GA47 O4](../overtures/ga47_2019__o4.md)** (recent "Declaration" mechanism). **Pruning:** the BCO 14-6 constitutional inquiries surfaced by keyword (GA10, GA50, GA52, GA32) were dropped — they construe committee authority, dissociation, and Stated-Clerk nomination, not the 14-6.k recommend-measures power O66 cites; no judicial case bears. **Outcome signal:** declaration overtures have a mixed record (GA21 O16, GA47 O4, GA19 O41 adopted; GA37 O18 negative; GA40 O10 answered by reference), so adoption is not automatic.

## O67 — Amend BCO 40-5 to Clarify a Court Shall Make Two Determinations before Citing a Lower Court
**Targets:** BCO 40-5 · **Source:** Potomac · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/03/Overture-67_Potomac_40-5.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/03/Overture-67_Potomac_40-5.pdf)

**What it does:** Amends BCO 40-5 so that, on receiving a report of important delinquency or grossly unconstitutional proceedings against a lower court, the higher court's "first step" is to make two threshold determinations — (1) whether the matter, if true, would be such a delinquency/violation, and (2) whether there is sufficient evidence from a credible source (e.g., BCO 31-8) — and only if both are answered Yes does it then cite the lower court to appear.

**Cites in its own grounds:** None (no prior cases, overtures, or inquiries by number). The grounds reason by analogy to BCO 31-2, BCO 31-8, Preliminary Principles 5 & 7, BCO 11-3, BCO 11-4, RAO 16-5, RAO 16-10.c, and OMSJC 15.

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
- **[2006-2 — Memorial re Louisiana Presbytery and TE J. Steven Wilkins](../cases/ga36_2008__2006-02.md)** (GA36/2008, other) — The Central Carolina memorial that launched the Wilkins/Louisiana 40-5 process; the central dispute was the threshold for invoking 40-5 against a presbytery, the very gateway this overture would formalize. [minutes](../markdown/ga36_2008.md#ga36-p75)
- **[2007-8 — Jones v. Louisiana Presbytery](../cases/ga36_2008__2007-08.md)** (GA36/2008, sustained) — SJC held the presbytery applied the wrong constitutional standard in deciding whether to proceed; bears on what a court must find before acting on an alleged delinquency. [minutes](../markdown/ga36_2008.md#ga36-p117)
- **[2008-14 — White v. Siouxlands Presbytery](../cases/ga38_2010__2008-14.md)** (GA38/2010, sustained) — Construes the 40-5 standard for whether a presbytery's handling of a credible report of delinquency was constitutional; directly on the citation-trigger question. [minutes](../markdown/ga38_2010.md#ga38-p137)
- **[2010-18/-19/-20/-21/-22/-23 — RPR citations re Review of Presbytery Records](../cases/ga39_2011__2010-18_2010-19_2010-20_2010-21_2010-22_2010-23.md)** (GA39/2011, administrative) — Six presbyteries cited via the RPR→40-5 route; bears directly on the overture's rationale §4 (how RPR should screen a 40-5 letter before citing). [minutes](../markdown/ga39_2011.md#ga39-p603)
- **[2012-10 — PCA v. Korean Capital Presbytery](../cases/ga41_2013__2012-10.md)** (GA41/2013, administrative) — A PCA-initiated 40-5 citation of a presbytery; illustrates the citation mechanic the overture would gate behind a threshold finding. [minutes](../markdown/ga41_2013.md#ga41-p618)
- **[2023-13 — BCO 40-5 Matter re Metropolitan NY](../cases/ga51_2024__2023-13.md)** (GA51/2024, remitted) — A recent contested 40-5 matter (decided with dissents) over how a court should proceed on a delinquency report; live friction at the gateway this overture addresses. ⭐ [minutes](../markdown/ga51_2024.md#ga51-p916)
- **[2023-14 — BCO 40-5 Matter re NW Georgia](../cases/ga51_2024__2023-14.md)** (GA51/2024, other) — Companion recent 40-5 matter on the same docket; same gateway question. ⭐ [minutes](../markdown/ga51_2024.md#ga51-p933)

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
- **34-35 IV** (GA34/2006) — Effect of eliminating "memorials" terminology on the pending Louisiana 40-5 case; bears on the procedural shape of how 40-5 matters are commenced and processed. [page](../inquiries/ga34_2006__ci07.md)
- **47th GA II.U** (GA47/2019) — CCB advice that the proposed amendments to BCO 40-4/40-5 clarifying the meaning of "credible report" were not in conflict with the Constitution; the "credible source / credible report" language is exactly what this overture's second determination codifies. [page](../inquiries/ga47_2019__ci21.md)
- **48th GA IV. Non-Judicial Reference 1** (GA48/2021) — CCB issued three opinions on procedure, anonymity, and standing when a presbytery receives a 40-5 report alleging delinquency by a Session; directly addresses the front-end screening this overture would require. ⭐ [page](../inquiries/ga48_2021__ci29.md)
- **51st GA II.W** (GA51/2024) — CCB found amending RAO 16-6.c.1 to remove its conflict with BCO 40-5 not in conflict with the BCO; relevant to the RAO/RPR machinery the overture's rationale §4 leans on. ⭐ [page](../inquiries/ga51_2024__ci23.md)

### Prior overtures
- **[GA47 O36](../overtures/ga47_2019__o36.md)** (2019, Approved → sent to presbyteries; ratification not located) — Savannah River's "Amend BCO 40-4 and 40-5 to Clarify the Meaning of 'Credible Report'" — the closest prior attempt to refine 40-5's trigger; this overture's determination #2 ("credible source") is the same project. [page](../markdown/ga47_2019.md#ga47-p684)
- **[GA51 O28](../overtures/ga51_2024__o28.md)** (2024, to CCB/OC) — New Jersey's "Amend RAO 16-6.c.1 to Eliminate Conflict with BCO 40-5"; companion-rules cleanup at the RAO/40-5 seam invoked by the overture's RPR rationale. ⭐ [page](../markdown/ga51_2024.md#ga51-p1180)
- **[GA37 O7](../overtures/ga37_2009__o7.md)** (2009, to CCB/OC) — Southeast Louisiana's "Declare SJC Manual Section 16 Unconstitutional and Request SJC to Amend It"; the SJC Manual §16 / OMSJC 15 memorial-and-citation procedure is the same machinery the overture cites (OMSJC 15) and would reshape. [page](../markdown/ga37_2009.md#ga37-p205)

### RPR exceptions
None found.

### Note
Heavily pruned. The provision-exact spine returned 60+ BCO 40-5 hits, but the overwhelming majority are routine complaints/appeals/references that merely cite 40-5 in passing or apply it to unrelated disciplinary facts (e.g., Chappell, Newton, Smith, Lachman, the Thompson/Granada series, Speck, Turner, Bulkeley, Gleason, etc.) — they do not construe the *threshold* question of what a court must determine *before* citing a lower court, and are omitted as incidental. Retained are actions bearing on (a) the gateway/standard for invoking 40-5 against a court (the Wilkins/Louisiana saga, White, the recent Metro NY / NW Georgia matters) and (b) the RPR→RAO→40-5 citation machinery the overture's rationale §4 expressly relies on (the 2010 RPR citations, 2012-10, GA51 O28 / II.W). The single most on-point bearing action is **GA47 O36 / II.U** — the prior attempt to define "credible report" in 40-4/40-5, the same word and purpose as this overture's second determination; drafters should reconcile with it. No renumbering affects BCO 40-5 (absent from bco_renumberings.jsonl). Pre-SJC GA12 (1984) hits and several bare "BCO 40-5 report/matter" docket lines lacked case pages and added no construal, so they were pruned. RPR-by-provision returned no BCO 40-5 exceptions (spine rpr=[]).

## O68 — Amend BCO 14-1 to Make AC Members Appointed by Committees and Agencies Non-voting
**Targets:** BCO 14-1 (specifically 14-1.12) · **Source:** Catawba Valley · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-68_CatawbaVly_14-1-1.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-68_CatawbaVly_14-1-1.pdf)

**What it does:** Amends BCO 14-1.12 (and conforming RAO 5-1) so the Administrative Committee consists of eleven voting members elected by the GA plus one *non-voting* representative from each of the nine program committees/agencies (CDM, CC, CTS, MNA, MTW, PCAF, Geneva, RUF, RH), who keep the privilege of the floor but lose the vote. Goal: confine AC voting authority to members directly elected by the Assembly.

**Cites in its own grounds:** None. The Whereas clauses argue solely from accountability/parity principles and cite no prior case, overture, or inquiry.

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
None found.
*(Spine returned Judicial Case 32-18 [GA22] and an SJC decision at GA24 p.81, both merely citing "14-1" on unrelated judicial matters — pruned as incidental; neither construes AC composition or committee-member voting.)*

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
- **GA52 II.F** (2025) — CCB found the proposed amendment making AC members from committees/agencies non-voting advisory members **not in conflict** with the Constitution (Adopted 8-0-0). This is the CCB review of the immediate predecessor of this very overture. ⭐ [page](../inquiries/ga52_2025__ci06.md)
- **GA51 II.Z** (2024) — CCB found a proposed BCO 14-1 amendment on permanent-committee/agency policy not in conflict (Adopted 8-0-0); directly on amending BCO 14-1's committee structure. ⭐ [page](../inquiries/ga51_2024__ci26.md)
- **GA47 III.B** (2019) — CCB advised a committee member who completed a full term is not eligible for consecutive service on a different committee/agency board without a sabbatical; construes membership rules of BCO 14-1.12, the subsection this overture rewrites. [page](../inquiries/ga47_2019__ci23.md)
- **GA47 III.A** (2019) — CCB advised an SJC member may serve concurrently on a GA agency board; construes BCO 14-1.12 committee/agency-membership interplay. [page](../inquiries/ga47_2019__ci22.md)
- **GA47 II.G / II.J / II.O / II.P / II.R** (2019) — CCB found a cluster of presbytery overtures amending BCO 14-1.10/.11/.12 (to allow non-ordained persons on GA committees/boards) **in conflict**; bears as prior CCB review of who may compose GA committee/agency membership under the same subsections. [G](../inquiries/ga47_2019__ci07.md) · [J](../inquiries/ga47_2019__ci10.md) · [O](../inquiries/ga47_2019__ci15.md) · [P](../inquiries/ga47_2019__ci16.md) · [R](../inquiries/ga47_2019__ci18.md)
- **28-19 III.3** (2000) — CCB clarified which GA entities the permanent-committee ineligibility rule reaches (cites BCO 14-1.12); bears on the membership/parity logic of 14-1.12. [page](../inquiries/ga28_2000__ci03.md)

*(Pruned as incidental: 30-29 III [SJC abolition], 34-34 II.C & GA46 App.O II.F [BCO 14-1.15 overture-routing], 30-29 Item 2 [14-1.4 health coverage], GA49 Suppl. III.2 & GA52 Suppl. II.2 [Stated-Clerk floor nominations] — none construe AC composition or committee-member voting.)*

### Prior overtures
- **[GA52 O9](../overtures/ga52_2025__o9.md)** (2025, Answered in the negative) — James River Presbytery, the immediate predecessor: same proposal to make AC members appointed by committees/agencies non-voting. This overture is a near-verbatim re-run. ⭐ [p.1349](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p1347)
- **[GA51 O31](../overtures/ga51_2024__o31.md)** (2024, Answered in the negative) — New River Presbytery, amend BCO 14-1 re permanent-committee & agency policy changes. ⭐ [p.1278](../markdown/ga51_2024.md#ga51-p1271)
- **[GA51 O32](../overtures/ga51_2024__o32.md)** (2024, Carried over) — Eastern Pennsylvania Presbytery, BCO 14-1 amendment (to CCB/OC/AC/CC...). ⭐ [p.1279](../markdown/ga51_2024.md#ga51-p1272)
- **[GA47 O8](../overtures/ga47_2019__o8.md)** (2019, Answered in the negative) — Ohio Valley, amend BCO 14-1.10/.11/.12 on who composes GA committees/boards. [p.603](../markdown/ga47_2019.md#ga47-p601)
- **[GA47 O19](../overtures/ga47_2019__o19.md)** (2019, Answered by reference) — Rocky Mountain, same 14-1.10/.11/.12 composition amendment. [p.633](../markdown/ga47_2019.md#ga47-p631)
- **[GA47 O21](../overtures/ga47_2019__o21.md)** (2019, Answered by reference) — Nashville, same 14-1.10/.11/.12 composition amendment. [p.641](../markdown/ga47_2019.md#ga47-p639)
- **[GA47 O32](../overtures/ga47_2019__o32.md)** (2019, Answered by reference) — Tennessee Valley, same 14-1.10/.11/.12 composition amendment. [p.666](../markdown/ga47_2019.md#ga47-p664)
- **[GA46 O26](../overtures/ga46_2018__o26.md)** (2018, Approved → sent to presbyteries) — Tennessee Valley, amend BCO 14-1.11 to allow non-ordained Covenant College trustees; prior change to committee/agency membership rules. [p.724](../markdown/ga46_2018.md#ga46-p722)
- **[GA29 O1](../overtures/ga29_2001__o1.md)** (2001, Approved & ratified 2002) — Missouri, amend BCO 14-1(12) to increase committee size and extend terms; a successful prior amendment to the exact subsection this overture rewrites. [p.141](../markdown/ga29_2001.md#ga29-p139)
- **[GA19 O29](../overtures/ga19_1991__o29.md)** (1991, Answered by reference) — Louisiana, amend RAO or BCO 14-1 to **limit Administrative Committee membership**; closest historical analog to the AC-composition question. [p.61](../markdown/ga19_1991.md#ga19-p59)
- **[GA11 O4](../overtures/ga11_1983__o4.md)** (1983, Answered by reference) — Mid-Atlantic, amend BCO 14-1 on consecutive permanent-committee terms. [p.56](../markdown/ga11_1983.md#ga11-p56)
- **[GA10 O4](../overtures/ga10_1982__o4.md)** (1982, Referred) — Mid-Atlantic, amend BCO 14-1(12) on second consecutive terms. [p.45](../markdown/ga10_1982.md#ga10-p45)
- **[GA9 O26](../overtures/ga09_1981__o26.md)** (1981, Referred) — Mid-Atlantic, amend BCO 14-1(12) on second consecutive terms. [p.49](../markdown/ga09_1981.md#ga09-p49)

*(Pruned as incidental — cite BCO 14-1 only for unrelated matters: GA8 O16 & GA9 O22 & GA10 O2 [TE/RE voting balance], GA12 O43, GA17 O33/O42, GA19 O9, GA20 O6 [RAO 13-1 insertion], GA21 O3/O10/O19/O44, GA22 O2/O20/O36, GA24 O2/O23/O30, GA30 O6, GA32 O10, GA35 O13, GA40 O25/O28, GA42 O11, GA45 O3/O7, GA46 O4/O13, GA47 O1/O14/O27, GA48 O3/O14, GA51 O11, GA52 O18/O30/O44 — SJC, boundaries, evolution, paperless GA, byFaith, RUF manual, etc.)*

### RPR exceptions
None found.
*(Spine's RPR hits are for **RAO 14-1** [presbytery-minutes review], a different provision from **BCO 14-1**; pruned as a false provision match.)*

### Note
Direct predecessor: GA52 O9 (James River, 2025) proposed the identical change and was answered in the negative even though the CCB found it constitutional (GA52 II.F) — so the friction is policy, not constitutionality. The CCB has twice (GA51 II.Z, GA52 II.F) blessed BCO 14-1 committee-structure amendments as not-in-conflict, so a constitutionality objection is unlikely; the live question is whether the Assembly wants to strip the vote from program-committee/agency representatives. The spine was high-recall because BCO 14-1 is a large chapter (committees, SJC, nominations, terms, BCO-amendment routing); I kept only actions construing AC/committee-member composition, membership eligibility, or the .12 subsection, and pruned the rest. No renumbering applies — BCO 14-1 has retained its number; older actions cite the parenthetical form "14-1(12)" rather than "14-1.12" for the same subsection.

## O69 — Amend BCO 32-18 and 42-5 to Clarify the Contents of the Record of the Case in Judicial Cases
**Targets:** BCO 32-18, 42-5 · **Source:** Southwest Florida · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-69_SWFlorida_ROC.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-69_SWFlorida_ROC.pdf)

**What it does:** Reconciles and consolidates the scattered definition of the "Record of the Case" across the Rules of Discipline: 32-18 is restructured into lettered subsections and made to point to 42-5 for the definition, and 42-5 is rewritten to enumerate exactly what the clerk must collect and transmit on appeal (minutes of trial proceedings per 32-18 incl. a transcription, minutes of any 32-3/32-5 meetings, the notice of appeal, papers admitted before the close of trial, and minutes of any censure). Aim: make it easier for clerks to assemble a complete ROC and for higher courts to review.

**Cites in its own grounds:** None by case/overture/inquiry number. The rationale invokes only BCO 35-9 and "the 2025 General Assembly's adoption of last year's helpful proposed change to that provision" (= GA52 O40, amending 35-9 to record all parts of a trial).

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
- **[2019-3 — Crouse v. Northwest Georgia Presbytery](../cases/ga48_2021__2019-03.md)** (GA48/2021, sustained) — squarely construes BCO 32-18 and 42-5 together on what the Record of the Case must contain and on the absence of a hearing transcript; the cleanest recent adjudication of the gap O69 addresses. ⭐ [minutes](../markdown/ga48_2021.md#ga48-p709)
- **[2021-13 — Dudt v. Northwest Georgia Presbytery](../cases/ga49_2022__2021-13.md)** (GA49/2022, sustained) — turns on minute-keeping "procedures stated in BCO 32-18," whether the trial "with transcript" was completed as directed in 32-18, and a 32-18 violation; directly on the ROC/transcription duties O69 codifies. ⭐ [minutes](../markdown/ga49_2022.md#ga49-p909)
- **[2023-19 — Huffman v. Tennessee Valley Presbytery](../cases/ga51_2024__2023-19.md)** (GA51/2024, other) — discusses what may and may not be part of the proposed Record of the Case and the parties' role in establishing it; bears on the enumeration/transmission O69 clarifies. ⭐ [minutes](../markdown/ga51_2024.md#ga51-p959)
- **2023-06/2023-08 — Baird et al. v. Grace Presbytery** (GA51/2024, sustained) — cites both 32-18 and 42-5; recent ROC dispute. ⭐ [minutes](../markdown/ga51_2024.md#ga51-p796)
- **[2022-7 — Harrell et al. v. Covenant Presbytery](../cases/ga50_2023__2022-07.md)** (GA50/2023, sustained) — cites 42-5; ROC sufficiency on appeal. ⭐ [minutes](../markdown/ga50_2023.md#ga50-p860)
- **[2009-28 — Ruff v. Nashville Presbytery](../cases/ga39_2011__2009-28.md)** (GA39/2011, sustained) — repeatedly weighs whether "the Record of the Case" gave a full account; cites 42-5; classic ROC-completeness friction. [minutes](../markdown/ga39_2011.md#ga39-p569)
- **[2011-15 — Hahn v. Philadelphia Metro West](../cases/ga42_2014__2011-11_2011-12_2011-15_2011-16.md)** (GA43/2015, out of order) — addresses perfecting of the record of the case and the trial transcript; cites 32-18. [minutes](../markdown/ga43_2015.md#ga43-p588)
- **[2010-4 — Sartorious et al. v. Siouxlands Presbytery](../cases/ga39_2011__2010-04.md)** (GA39/2011, denied) — cites 32-18. [minutes](../markdown/ga39_2011.md#ga39-p580)
- **[2004-8 — Thornton v. Westminster Presbytery](../cases/ga34_2006__2004-08.md)** (GA34/2006, sustained) — cites 32-18 on the written record. [minutes](../markdown/ga34_2006.md#ga34-p87)

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
- **App. O II.D** (GA41/2013, not in conflict) — CCB found Suncoast Florida's overture defining supporting reasons "not in conflict if BCO 32-18 is read as addressing cases in process." Bears on how 32-18's ROC duties are read. [page](../inquiries/ga41_2013__ci01.md)

### Prior overtures
- **[GA22 O24](../overtures/ga22_1994__o24.md)** (1995, Approved & ratified) — "Amend BCO 32-18 to Clarify the Written Record of the Case" (Philadelphia). The original attempt at the same clarification O69 now extends. [page](../markdown/ga22_1994.md#ga22-p246)
- **[GA29 O15](../overtures/ga29_2001__o15.md)** (2002, Approved & ratified) — "Amend BCO 35-7 & 32-18 to Require Recording & Transcription of Testimony" (Central Carolina). Established the transcription duty O69's 42-5 references. [page](../markdown/ga29_2001.md#ga29-p141)
- **[GA41 O4](../overtures/ga41_2013__o4.md)** (2013, Answered in the negative) — "Amend BCO 32 by Adding Section 32-21 on Supporting Reasons for Appeal" (Suncoast Florida). Prior attempt to refine Chapter 32 appeal mechanics. [page](../markdown/ga41_2013.md#ga41-p824)
- **[GA41 O5](../overtures/ga41_2013__o5.md)** (2013, Answered in the negative) — "Amend BCO 42 by Adding 42-13 to Define Terms in Chapter 42" (Suncoast Florida). Same definitional impulse as O69, in the same chapter. [page](../markdown/ga41_2013.md#ga41-p825)

### RPR exceptions
- **BCO 32-18** — 2 citations: [South Texas](../rpr/exc/south-texas__035.md) (31st/2003, judicial-commission report missing copy of complaint, panel names, quorum — outstanding) and [Southwest Florida](../rpr/exc/southwest-florida__031.md) (36th/2008, "No 'record of the case' is appended" — closed satisfactory). The 2008 exception is from O69's own presbytery and is the exact ROC-completeness problem it targets. [by provision](../index/RPR-BY-PROVISION.md)
- **BCO 42-5** — 1 citation: [Warrior](../rpr/exc/warrior__050.md) (41st/2013, documentation concerning appeal not recorded in the minutes — raised/open). ROC-transmission friction. [by provision](../index/RPR-BY-PROVISION.md)

### Note
Cross-link: O69's own grounds rest on **[GA52 O40](../overtures/ga52_2025__o40.md)** (amend BCO 35-9 to record "all parts of a trial," adopted 2025) — O69 extends that recording duty into the ROC-definition machinery. Companion GA53 overtures in the same chapters: **O75** (BCO 42-4/42-5/42-6, Central Florida — appeal mechanics) and O85/O86 (appeals vs. complaints / dismissals / ROC). **Pruning:** the spine's CCB hit **II.U** (GA52/2025, BCO 36 censure-elevation, ga52_2025__ci21) lists 32-18 as only one of nine provisions in passing and concerns elevating a censure, not the ROC — pruned as incidental. **Link caveats:** the join supplied verbatim `case_page` deep-links for 2021-13, 2023-19, and 2011-15 (consolidated file); 2019-3 links to the cases directory file (ga48_2021__2019-03.md, confirmed extant); every other case carries its `../markdown` minutes anchor (also verbatim from the join) as the deep-link. Pruned as incidental: 2023-9 Myers v. Illiana Presbytery — BCO 32-18 appears only in a dissenting opinion listing many formal-process provisions as hypothetical examples; the holding concerns due process in censure elevation, not ROC definition. 2016-8 Doty v. Nashville Presbytery — BCO 32-18 appears in a dissent footnote listing 8 provisions about who draws up indictments; not about ROC contents. 1999-6 Shive v. Central Carolina — BCO 32-18 in metadata only, does not appear in the case text; case concerns excommunication/censure elevation. 1997-6 Fitzsimmons v. Evangel Presbytery — BCO 42-5 cited only as procedural filing reference ("Session filed its record of the case in accordance with BCO 42-5"); not construed on ROC contents. 1997-3 Nickoley v. Rocky Mountain — dismissed as administratively out of order without any analysis of 42-5. "Judicial Case 32-18" (GA22/1994, minutes link ga22-p246) — not a judicial case; the p246 anchor is a prior overture (GA22 O24, already captured in the Prior Overtures section above).
