## O70 — Expand Korean Northwest Boundaries to Include Alaska, Hawaii, Oregon, and Washington
**Targets:** (boundaries — non-provision overture) · **Source:** Korean Northwest Presbytery (to MNA) · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-70_KoreanNW_Boundaries.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-70_KoreanNW_Boundaries.pdf)

**What it does:** Asks GA53 to add the states of Alaska, Hawaii, Oregon, and Washington to the boundaries of Korean Northwest Presbytery, effective immediately. The grounds note that the 9 Korean Language Presbyteries currently cover 41 states, leaving 9 states unassigned, and that although these presbyteries are "non-geographical" relative to the wider PCA they are geographical relative to one another.

**Cites in its own grounds:** The 10th General Assembly's continuation of Korean Language Presbyteries since 1982 (M10GA, p. 92-93); and BCO 13-2 Editorial Comment (for the "non-geographical" status of the language presbyteries). No prior judicial cases or specific prior overtures are cited.

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
None found. The exact-provision spine returns nothing (provisions=[]). Topical search surfaced numerous Korean-presbytery cases (the Korean Capital Presbytery / KPCW discipline cases of 1999–2002, Kim v. Korean Southwest, etc.), but these are intra-presbytery discipline disputes that merely name Korean presbyteries as parties; none construe a presbytery-boundary or territorial question. Pruned as incidental. (A GA13 minutes excerpt describing Overture 21 to place the Hawaiian Islands outside Pacific Presbytery's boundaries is mis-indexed as a "case"; it is a legislative boundary action, not a judicial decision, and is treated under Prior overtures.)

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
- **CI 10-77** (GA10 / 1982) — Constitutionality of a non-geographical presbytery under BCO 11-4: the CCB found the BCO does not address non-geographical presbyteries, that BCO 11-4 implies geographical bounds while BCO 13-1 does not limit "bounds" geographically. This is the foundational ruling permitting the Korean Language Presbyteries that O70 relies on, and it frames exactly the "geographical vs. non-geographical bounds" tension O70 invokes. [page](../inquiries/ga10_1982__ci04.md)

### Prior overtures
- **[GA52 O2](../overtures/ga52_2025__o2.md)** (2025, Adopted final) — Expand Boundaries of South Florida Presbytery to Include Puerto Rico and US Virgin Islands. The most recent precedent for a presbytery expanding into new, previously-unassigned territory; adopted as final, showing the current GA's posture toward such extensions. ⭐ [p.1168](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p1166), [p.1359](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p1357)
- **[GA42 O25](../overtures/ga42_2014__o25.md)** (2014, Referred) — Expand Boundaries of Korean Southeastern Presbytery. The closest on-point precedent: a Korean Language Presbytery seeking to enlarge its geographic territory. Outcome (Referred, to MNA) shows such requests are routed through MNA rather than adopted on the floor. [p.81](../markdown/ga42_2014.md#ga42-p79), [p.827](../markdown/ga42_2014.md#ga42-p825), [p.888](../markdown/ga42_2014.md#ga42-p886)
- **[GA42 O26](../overtures/ga42_2014__o26.md)** (2014, Referred) — Divide Korean Southwest Presbytery into Two Presbyteries. Companion 2014 action reorganizing Korean Language Presbytery geography; same referral disposition. [p.81](../markdown/ga42_2014.md#ga42-p79), [p.828](../markdown/ga42_2014.md#ga42-p826), [p.888](../markdown/ga42_2014.md#ga42-p886)
- **[GA39 O5](../overtures/ga39_2011__o5.md)** (2011, Adopted final) — Divide Korean Eastern Presbytery to Create Korean Northeastern Presbytery. Shows the GA does adopt geographic reorganizations of the Korean Language Presbyteries (here creating the Korean Northeastern named in O70's whereas list). [p.80](../markdown/ga39_2011.md#ga39-p78), [p.620](../markdown/ga39_2011.md#ga39-p618), [p.679](../markdown/ga39_2011.md#ga39-p677)
- **[GA10 O21](../overtures/ga10_1982__o21.md)** (1982, Adopted final) — Extend Siouxlands Presbytery Boundaries to Cover Five-State Region. A directly analogous mechanism — extending a presbytery's bounds across multiple states — adopted in the same Assembly that originated the Korean Language Presbyteries (M10GA, cited in O70's grounds). [p.49](../markdown/ga10_1982.md#ga10-p49)

### RPR exceptions
None found. The exact-provision spine returns nothing. BCO 13-2 carries 71 RPR exceptions, but every one concerns teaching elders "laboring out of bounds" without the required concurrence (e.g., [Korean Capital](../rpr/korean-capital.md) 34th/2006; [Grace](../rpr/grace.md) 51st/2024) — a TE-labor question, not the territorial-boundary question O70 raises. Pruned as incidental. [by provision](../index/RPR-BY-PROVISION.md)

### Note
Non-provision (boundaries) overture, so the deterministic join spine is empty and all bearing actions come from topical search of the index (OVERTURES.md, INQUIRIES.md, cases.jsonl). No renumbering caveat applies (BCO 13-2 is stable). Pruning: all Korean-presbytery judicial cases and all BCO 13-2 RPR exceptions were dropped as incidental — they name Korean presbyteries / cite BCO 13-2 but address discipline or out-of-bounds labor, not presbytery territory. The prior first pass also asserted two boundary "cases" (a "2010-20" and an "In re Korean Northwest Presbytery, GA46") that do not appear in the join output or the index search; they are not carried forward. The genuinely bearing line is the chain of Korean Language Presbytery geographic reorganizations (GA39 O5, GA42 O25/O26), the GA10 constitutional grounding (CI 10-77), and the recent territorial-expansion precedent (GA52 O2). Procedurally significant: prior Korean-presbytery boundary requests (GA42 O25/O26) were Referred to MNA, whereas the recent South Florida expansion (GA52 O2) was Adopted as final — disposition has turned on MNA handling, not any constitutional bar. Companion GA53 boundary overtures should be cross-checked for the other unspecified states.

---

## O71 — Amend BCO 5-9.e, 9-2, and 9-7 to Allow Session to Directly Administer Diaconal Ministry
**Targets:** BCO 5-9.e, 9-2, 9-7 · **Source:** Northern California Presbytery · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-71_NCal_DiaconalMinistry.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-71_NCal_DiaconalMinistry.pdf)

**What it does:** Lets a Session, with three-quarters congregational ratification, directly administer diaconal ministry in lieu of electing deacons, and appoint unordained, non-elected lay volunteers (men and women) to assist — expressly forbidding that they be called deacon/deaconess or be ordained or installed as officers; conforms 5-9.e and 9-7 accordingly.

**Cites in its own grounds:** None (cites only Scripture — Titus 1:5, Phil 1:1, 1 Tim 3, Acts 6, Acts 20:17 — plus BCO 9-1 and a Ramsay / Morton Smith quotation; no prior cases, overtures, or inquiries).

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
- **[2009-25/2009-26 — Brown v. Northern California Presbytery / Session of Grace PC v. Northern California Presbytery](../cases/ga39_2011__2009-25_2009-26.md)** (GA39/2011, sustained) — Same presbytery as O71; the SJC adjudicated NorCal's permitted views on the diaconate and how diaconal ministry may be organized, directly construing BCO 9-2/9-7. Most on-point precedent. [minutes](../markdown/ga39_2011.md#ga39-p550)
- **[2011-14 — Reese and Bech v. Philadelphia Presbytery](../cases/ga42_2014__2011-14.md)** (GA42/2014, sustained) — Construes the office of deacon under BCO 9-2 in the context of a candidate's refusal to ordain men as deacons and use of a "mercy" model — bears on whether diaconal function may be detached from the ordained office. [minutes](../markdown/ga42_2014.md#ga42-p530)
- **[Case 2007-13 — Kniseley v. Rocky Mountain](../cases/ga37_2009__2007-13.md)** (GA37/2009, denied) — Addresses who may be a member of a "diaconate" and restricts the term, construing BCO 9-2/9-7 on diaconal membership and the elder/deacon two-office structure. [minutes](../markdown/ga39_2011.md#ga39-p557)

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
- **38-34 II.E** (GA38/2010) — From Northern California Presbytery itself; CCB found an overture appointing unordained persons to diaconal ministry in conflict (it implied an unordained office contrary to BCO 17-1). The precise design O71 now attempts, and a prior NorCal attempt — O71's "no lay volunteer … called deacon/deaconess … not ordained or installed" wording appears engineered to answer this conflict. [page](../inquiries/ga38_2010__ci04.md)
- **38-34 II.A** (GA38/2010) — CCB found an overture prohibiting deaconesses in conflict because "deaconess" need not denote an ordained office; frames the 9-7 boundary O71 works within. [page](../inquiries/ga38_2010__ci02.md)
- **38-34 II.D** (GA38/2010) — CCB found an overture prohibiting commissioned/installed assistants to deacons in conflict on the same grounds; O71 likewise creates unordained assistants but forbids commissioning/installing them. [page](../inquiries/ga38_2010__ci03.md)
- **App. O II.H** (GA46/2018) — CCB found Grace Presbytery's deaconess/assistants overture in conflict, holding the Session (not the congregation) is the appointing body requiring vows; bears on O71's congregational-ratification mechanism and Session appointment of volunteers. [page](../inquiries/ga46_2018__ci04.md)
- **II.Q** (GA47/2019) — CCB found Metro New York's overture letting individual sessions decide locally whether women may serve as deacons NOT in conflict; closest favorable analog to O71's local-Session-discretion structure (BCO 9-3, 7-2). [page](../inquiries/ga47_2019__ci17.md)

### Prior overtures
- **[GA52 O34](../overtures/ga52_2025__o34.md)** (2025, Adopted) — Amended RAO 16 to require reporting on session and diaconate membership and duties; touches BCO 9-2 diaconate structure. ⭐ [page](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p1270)
- **[GA47 O40](../overtures/ga47_2019__o40.md)** (2019, —) — Urged sessions to acknowledge/support women leaders under BCO 9-7; same provision and same unordained-women-in-diaconal-work concern. [page](../markdown/ga47_2019.md#ga47-p692)
- **[GA46 O9](../overtures/ga46_2018__o9.md)** (2018, Approved → sent to presbyteries; ratification not located) — Grace Presbytery's amendment of BCO 9-7 (and new 24-11) on women serving as deaconesses; a prior attempt to reshape 9-7's assistants language. [page](../markdown/ga46_2018.md#ga46-p684)
- **[GA38 O2](../overtures/ga38_2010__o2.md)** (2010, —) — Central Carolina's amend BCO 9-7 to prohibit deaconesses; directly construes 9-7's "godly men and women" assistants clause that O71 edits. [page](../markdown/ga38_2010.md#ga38-p386)
- **[GA38 O7](../overtures/ga38_2010__o7.md)** (2010, Adopted) — Evangel's "Reconsider Ordination of Women to the Office of Deacon"; framed the GA38 diaconate debate behind O71. [page](../markdown/ga38_2010.md#ga38-p384)
- **[GA38 O9](../overtures/ga38_2010__o9.md)** (2010, —) — Eastern Carolina's revise BCO 9-7 to prohibit commissioning assistants to deacons as office bearers; mirror-image of O71's "not officers" assistants clause. [page](../markdown/ga38_2010.md#ga38-p387)
- **[GA38 O13](../overtures/ga38_2010__o13.md)** (2010, —) — Westminster's prohibit electing/installing assistants to deacons as office bearers; same 9-7 assistants question. [page](../markdown/ga38_2010.md#ga38-p389)

### RPR exceptions
- **BCO 9-7** — 3 citations (e.g., Metro Atlanta, GA38/2010: practice #4 quoting BCO 9-7 on the Session selecting assistants to deacons, unsatisfactory/outstanding) — real-world friction over Sessions appointing diaconal assistants, the exact mechanism O71 codifies. [by provision](../index/RPR-BY-PROVISION.md)
- **BCO 9-2** — 2 citations (both Metro Atlanta, GA38/2010: practices denying the BCO provision for men leading the diaconate, election by the congregation) — bears on O71's shift of diaconal administration to the Session and away from congregational election. [by provision](../index/RPR-BY-PROVISION.md)
- **BCO 5-9** — 22 citations, but all concern particularization/officer-election procedure (e.g., Northern California GA35/36; deacons commissioned without record of election/ordination) rather than 5-9.e's devolution-on-the-Session clause O71 edits; retained only as background. [by provision](../index/RPR-BY-PROVISION.md)

### Note
Pruned as incidental spine hits: the three BCO 5-9 judicial cases — **2020-6 Gordon v. Southern New England** (demission/credentials), **2022-23 Woodham v. South Florida** (demission), and **2023-11 Psiaki v. Pacific Northwest** (eligibility to vote in officer elections) — each cite BCO 5-9 only in passing and do not construe 5-9.e's "duties devolve upon the Session" clause. Also pruned: CCB **52 II.W** (RAO 16 reporting, only tangentially BCO 9-2) and the four pre-2000 title-matched prior overtures (GA10 O17 trustees/deacon duties, GA19 O40, GA21 O5 officer-training, GA22 O36) returned by body+title matching but not bearing on the deacon-administration question. Inquiry **27-43 II.1** (deacon/session authority to sell donated property) was pruned as off-topic (property disposition, not office structure). No renumbering affects BCO 5-9, 9-2, or 9-7 (none found in bco_renumberings.jsonl). Strongest bearing actions: the GA38 deaconess/assistants cluster (II.A/D/E and overtures O2/O9/O13) — note II.E and an earlier overture both came from Northern California, O71's own presbytery, and were found in conflict — plus the favorable GA47 II.Q precedent on local-Session discretion. This first deterministic pass corrects the earlier draft, which cited non-deep-link placeholders ([CCB-OVERTURE-ADVICE.md](../index/CCB-OVERTURE-ADVICE.md), [INQUIRIES.md](../index/INQUIRIES.md)) and overtures absent from the provision spine (GA46 O25, GA45 O8); all citations here are copied verbatim from the join output.

---

## O72 — Add a new BCO 12-8 to Require Recording of Session and Diaconate Members in Session Minutes
**Targets:** BCO 12-8 (new; renumbers old 12-8→12-9, 12-9→12-10) · **Source:** Ascension · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-72_Ascension_12.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-72_Ascension_12.pdf)

**What it does:** Adds a new BCO 12-8 requiring every Session to annually record in its minutes a list of all persons comprising the Session and the Diaconate; if the church has no Diaconate, the minutes must state why and whether those duties have devolved upon the Session under BCO 9-2. Aimed at presbytery "review and control" and at surfacing churches that have foregone ordaining deacons; deliberately mirrors the language of BCO 12-7.

**Cites in its own grounds:** The GA52 (2025, Chattanooga) "similar overture" that was defeated — it sought to amend the RAO and failed the 2/3 threshold but drew a majority (929–730). O72 routes the same change through the BCO (not the RAO) to answer the procedural objection that sank the prior version. Also references BCO Preface, 9-2, and 12-7 (provisions, not actions).

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
None found.

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
None found.

### Prior overtures
- **[GA52 O34](../overtures/ga52_2025__o34.md)** (2025, failed 929–730, did not meet 2/3) — "Amend RAO 16 to Require Reporting on Session and Diaconate Membership and Duties." ⭐ The "similar overture" O72's rationale expressly cites and answers: the same session/diaconate-reporting change, attempted via the RAO last year and defeated on the 2/3 RAO-amendment threshold; O72 re-engineers it into the BCO. (The corpus overtures table labels it "Adopted (final)," but the GA52 minutes record the RAO amendment itself as **failed (929-730)** — the disposition O72 relies on.) [page](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p1270)
- **[GA46 O25](../overtures/ga46_2018__o25.md)** (2018, Answered in the negative) — "Address the Unordained Diaconate" (Savannah River). Earlier attempt at the underlying concern O72 invokes (churches foregoing ordained deacons); topically related, not a prior version of the recording mechanism. [page](../markdown/ga46_2018.md#ga46-p774)

### RPR exceptions
- **BCO 12-8** — 2 citations: [Houston Metro](../rpr/exc/houston-metro__026.md), 47th (2019), "No record of review of records of church sessions" (satisfactory, closed); [Ascension](../rpr/exc/ascension__011.md), 48th (2021), improperly citing two Sessions with an exception of substance (satisfactory, closed). These cite the *current* 12-8 (annual statistical records, which O72 renumbers to 12-9), not the new recording duty, but show the review-and-control machinery O72 mirrors is actively exercised. [by provision](../index/RPR-BY-PROVISION.md)

### Note
The provision-exact spine for the new BCO 12-8 returned no judicial cases, inquiries, or CCB advice and only the 2 RPR rows above — expected, since 12-8 does not yet exist and the spine is provision-exact. The two prior overtures are a topical supplement (STEP 3): GA52 O34 is the directly bearing predecessor named in O72's own grounds (link to the GA52 minutes, where the RAO amendment failed 929-730), and GA46 O25 is a looser topical match on the unordained-diaconate concern. Pruned from a looser first pass: "CCB ci23," "Inquiry 22-13," and "Inquiry 30-29" — none appear in the deterministic join for BCO 12-8 nor are cited in the overture's grounds, and they lacked verifiable corpus deep-links, so they are dropped. GA53 context: O72 sits beside a diaconate cluster (O34 amend 9-2 on establishing a diaconate; O36/O38 on elder/deacon duties; O37 women deacons) and a session-records cluster, but its recording requirement is distinct.

---

## O73 — Amend RAO 4-9 to Require 2/3 Majority to Elect Stated Clerk and Coordinators after 3 Consecutive Years of Service
**Targets:** RAO 4-9 · **Source:** TE Cody Hooper (to CCB, OC, AC, CDM, MNA, MTW, RUF) · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-73_TEHooper_RAO4-9.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-73_TEHooper_RAO4-9.pdf)

**What it does:** Amends RAO 4-9 so that once a nominee for Stated Clerk or program-Committee coordinator has served three consecutive years in his position, his re-election in each successive year requires a two-thirds vote of those present and voting (rather than a simple majority); the annual-election and examination-before-first-employment provisions are otherwise retained. Stated purpose: prevent de facto lifetime appointments and give the Assembly a means to transition leaders when serious concerns arise, by analogy to BCO 20-5.

**Cites in its own grounds:** None — cites only constitutional provisions (BCO 14-1, BCO 20-5, RAO 4-9), not prior cases, overtures, or inquiries.

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
None found.

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
- **Supplemental III.1** (GA49/2022) — Whether Committees of Commissioners may nominate substitute program coordinators; CCB ruled a CoC may only approve or disapprove nominees for program coordinator and has no authority to nominate substitutes. Construes the RAO 4-9 annual-election nomination machinery this overture amends. ⭐ [page](../inquiries/ga49_2022__ci29.md)
- **Supplemental III.2** (GA49/2022) — Floor nomination procedure for the office of Stated Clerk; CCB advised floor nominations follow the same procedure as other contested offices and nominees must be examined by the TEC. Bears on the RAO 4-9 election/examination process the overture revises. ⭐ [page](../inquiries/ga49_2022__ci30.md)
- **Supplemental II.2** (GA52/2025) — Floor nominations for Stated Clerk when the AC brings no nominee; CCB ruled floor nominations are permitted under RAO 3-4 even if the AC brings no Stated Clerk nominee. ⭐ Recent; construes the RAO 4-9 Stated-Clerk election that the overture would raise to a 2/3 threshold. [page](../inquiries/ga52_2025__ci35.md)

### Prior overtures
- **[GA39 O2](../overtures/ga39_2011__o2.md)** (2011, Answered in the negative) — Amend RAO 4-9 to Set Term Limits for Program Committee Coordinators and Stated Clerk. Direct prior attempt to constrain the same RAO 4-9 election (by term limits); failed. [page](../markdown/ga39_2011.md#ga39-p77)
- **[GA19 O43](../overtures/ga19_1991__o43.md)** (1991, Answered in the negative) — Amend RAO 4-9 to Limit Coordinators & Stated Clerk to Two Four-Year Terms. Earliest direct attempt to limit tenure under RAO 4-9; failed — and authored by the same Presbytery of the Ascension that rejected O73. [page](../markdown/ga19_1991.md#ga19-p60)
- **[GA15 O37](../overtures/ga15_1987__o37.md)** (1987, Adopted) — Amend RAO Article III on GA Coordinator and Stated Clerk Selection. Topical supplement (predates current numbering); shaped the coordinator/Stated-Clerk election scheme now codified in RAO 4-9. [page](../markdown/ga15_1987.md#ga15-p42)
- **[GA12 O38](../overtures/ga12_1984__o38.md)** (1984, Answered in the negative) — Require GA Coordinator Candidates to Be Examined Before Election. Topical supplement; bears on the examination-before-election clause carried in RAO 4-9 (which this overture retains). [page](../markdown/ga12_1984.md#ga12-p57)

### RPR exceptions
None found.

### Note
The provision-exact join returned RAO 4-9 hits only; no judicial cases or RPR exceptions cite RAO 4-9, consistent with it being a procedural rule (Rules of Assembly Operations), not a justiciable BCO provision. No pruning was needed on the spine — all three inquiries genuinely construe the RAO 4-9 election/nomination machinery, and both spine overtures (GA39 O2, GA19 O43) are squarely on point as failed prior attempts to constrain the same election. Topical supplement (Step 3a) added GA15 O37 and GA12 O38 from /workspace/index/OVERTURES.md, which the provision-exact join missed because they predate the "RAO 4-9" label (they cite RAO Article III / coordinator-examination). No BCO renumbering applies — bco_renumberings.jsonl covers BCO chapters only, not the RAO. Note the unusual posture: O73 was rejected by its own Presbytery of the Ascension and sent to GA by an individual TE under RAO 11-10; that same presbytery authored the earliest term-limit attempt, GA19 O43.

---

## O74 — Add a New Chapter BCO 17A 'Of Commissioning for Non-Ordained Ministry'
**Targets:** BCO 17A (new chapter) · **Source:** E Carolina · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-74_ECar_17A.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-74_ECar_17A.pdf)

**What it does:** Adds a new chapter (17A) creating a constitutional category of "commissioning," by which a Session or Presbytery may publicly set apart a qualified member — explicitly "men or women" — for a non-ordained ministry role (teaching, discipleship, mercy, leadership, administration, counseling) without conferring ordained office. It builds in safeguards that commissioning may not create new offices, confer ruling/teaching authority, or blur BCO 7 and 8.

**Cites in its own grounds:** No prior cases, overtures, or inquiries. The grounds cite only Scripture (Acts 13:1–3; 14:23; 15:22, 27, 32; etc.) and constitutional text BCO 7-2, 17-1, and BCO 7 and 8 generally.

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
None found. (The exact-provision spine returned no provisions for a new chapter; topical search of cases.jsonl synopsis/topics for deaconess / unordained / commissioning surfaced no SJC or CJB case — this question has historically been settled by overture and CCB advice, not litigation.)

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
- **38-34 II.E** (GA38/2010) — CCB found Northern California's overture appointing unordained men and women to diaconal ministry roles in conflict, partly because it implied an unordained office contrary to BCO 17-1 — the most on-point precedent against a constitutional "non-ordained ministry" category. [page](../inquiries/ga38_2010__ci04.md)
- **38-34 II.A** (GA38/2010) — CCB held "deaconess" need not denote an ordained office equivalent to deacon (BCO 9-7); bears on whether commissioning women is constitutionally permissible. [page](../inquiries/ga38_2010__ci02.md)
- **38-34 II.D** (GA38/2010) — CCB found an overture prohibiting commissioned/installed assistants to deacons in conflict, on the same BCO 9-7 grounds; bears directly on commissioning non-ordained assistants. [page](../inquiries/ga38_2010__ci03.md)
- **46 II.H** (GA46/2018) — CCB found Grace Presbytery's deaconess/women-officer overture in conflict, noting the Session (not congregation) is the appointing body and vows are required (BCO 9-7, 11-2, 24-11); bears on O74's Session/Presbytery authorization mechanism. [page](../inquiries/ga46_2018__ci04.md)
- **47 II.Q** (GA47/2019) — CCB found Metro New York's overture letting local sessions decide whether women may serve as deacons NOT in conflict (BCO 7-2, 9-3, 17-3); a key data point that some women-in-service schemes pass CCB review. [page](../inquiries/ga47_2019__ci17.md)
- **50 II.S** (GA50/2023) — CCB found amending BCO 7-3 to regulate titling of unordained persons not in conflict; bears on the "what may an unordained commissioned person be called" boundary O74 raises. ⭐ [page](../inquiries/ga50_2023__ci19.md)
- **51 II.J** (GA51/2024) — CCB found amending BCO 7-2 to limit ordination to biological males not in conflict; frames the ordination/non-ordination line O74 invokes. ⭐ [page](../inquiries/ga51_2024__ci10.md)
- **12-53 III,69** (GA12/1984) — CCB advised that believing Scripture permits women deacons (while abiding by BCO in practice) is not alone grounds to deny ordination (BCO 7-2, 9-3, 21-5); early construal of the same office/non-office tension. [page](../inquiries/ga12_1984__ci09.md)

### Prior overtures
- **[GA6 O5](../overtures/ga06_1978__o5.md)** (1978) — "Add BCO Language Authorizing Sessions to Commission Non-Ordained Church Workers" (Western Carolinas) — the nearest prior attempt at exactly O74's reform; outcome not recorded in the index. [page](../markdown/ga06_1978.md#ga06-p35)
- **[GA38 O10](../overtures/ga38_2010__o10.md)** (2010, Answered in the negative) — Amend BCO 1-4, 4-2, 5-10, 7-2, 9-2, 9-7 and add 9-8 for Unordained Diaconal Ministry (Northern California) — a comprehensive unordained-ministry framework rejected by the Assembly; closely parallels O74's design and was the basis of CCB 38-34 II.E. [page](../markdown/ga38_2010.md#ga38-p392)
- **[GA38 O16](../overtures/ga38_2010__o16.md)** (2010) — "Affirm the Permissibility of Unordained Deaconesses in the PCA" (Tennessee Valley) — affirmative companion to the 2010 cluster. [page](../markdown/ga38_2010.md#ga38-p390)
- **[GA38 O2](../overtures/ga38_2010__o2.md)** (2010) — "Amend BCO 9-7 to Prohibit Deaconesses" (Central Carolina) — the contrary side of the 2010 debate; basis of CCB 38-34 II.A. [page](../markdown/ga38_2010.md#ga38-p386)
- **[GA46 O25](../overtures/ga46_2018__o25.md)** (2018, Answered in the negative) — "Address the Unordained Diaconate" (Savannah River) — directly about formalizing unordained service; rejected. [page](../markdown/ga46_2018.md#ga46-p774)
- **[GA46 O9](../overtures/ga46_2018__o9.md)** (2018, Approved → presbyteries; ratification not located) — Amend BCO 9-7 and add 24-11 re Women Serving as Deaconesses (Grace) — passed the floor but did not ratify; basis of CCB 46 II.H. [page](../markdown/ga46_2018.md#ga46-p684)
- **[GA50 O26](../overtures/ga50_2023__o26.md)** (2023, Approved & ratified 2024) — Amend BCO 7-3 to Prohibit Ecclesiastical Titles for Unordained People (Northwest Georgia) — the only one of this family that became constitutional text; constrains what a commissioned non-ordained person may be titled, a live tension for O74. ⭐ [page](../markdown/ga50_2023.md#ga50-p1028)
- **[GA51 O29](../overtures/ga51_2024__o29.md)** (2024, Answered by reference) — Amend BCO 53 to Prohibit Women from Preaching in Chapel and Campus Ministry Services (Bryce Avenue) — bounds the teaching/preaching roles O74 would open to commissioned women. ⭐ [page](../markdown/ga51_2024.md#ga51-p1182)
- **[GA12 O28](../overtures/ga12_1984__o28.md)** (1984, Answered in the negative) — "Study the Question of Women Serving in the Diaconate" (Delmarva) — earliest GA-level engagement with women in formal service. [page](../markdown/ga12_1984.md#ga12-p44)

### RPR exceptions
None found. (Spine returned no provisions, so no provision-keyed RPR rows; a new chapter has no presbytery records-of-proceedings exception history.) [by provision](../index/RPR-BY-PROVISION.md)

### Note
Companion GA53 overtures on the same axis: **O14** (SWFL) and **O48** (NWGA), both amending BCO 7-2/7-3/9-7 on titles/commissioning of unordained persons, and **O37** (Pacific) to allow women to serve as ordained deacons — O74 should be read alongside these (it takes the "new category" route rather than amending existing office chapters). Renumbering: BCO chapter 17 has NOT been renumbered, so no old-number search was needed. Pruning: the high-recall topical sweep surfaced many incidental hits I dropped — GA "commissioner" allotment/parity overtures (BCO 14-2) and judicial-"commission" CCB inquiries (BCO 15) use the word "commission" in unrelated senses; women-in-combat resolutions, women on GA agency committees/boards (BCO 14-1), and the women-preaching-in-worship line (BCO 12-5/53) touch adjacent questions but do not construe the ordination/commissioning distinction O74 creates, so they were excluded except where (GA51 O29) they directly bound the roles O74 enables.

---

## O75 — Amend BCO 42 to Clarify the Process for Filing an Appeal
**Targets:** BCO 42-4, 42-5, 42-6 · **Source:** Central Florida Presbytery · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-75_CFL_42.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-75_CFL_42.pdf)

**What it does:** Rewrites BCO 42-4 to delete the separate "notice of appeal" step, making clear the single required step is filing the "written appeal with supporting reasons" with both clerks within 30 days of notification of the last court's decision; conforms 42-5 (Record of the Case duty runs from receipt of the written appeal) and 42-6 (the suspending effect now attaches to "the filing of the written appeal" rather than to "notice of appeal").

**Cites in its own grounds:** None (the overture argues from the documentary history of BCO 42 — 1858, 1867, 1869, 1879, 1925, and the ~1984 introduction of "notice of appeal" — but cites no SJC case, inquiry, or prior overture by number).

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
- **[2004-09 — Appeal of RE Robar v. Central Carolina](../cases/ga33_2005__2004-09.md)** (GA33/2005, dismissed) — found judicially out of order for not being "properly filed according to BCO 42-4"; squarely construes the filing requirement the overture rewrites, including the notice-of-appeal vs. written-appeal distinction. [minutes](../markdown/ga33_2005.md#ga33-p145)
- **[2016-02 — Robertstad v. North Texas Presbytery](../cases/ga45_2017__2016-02.md)** (GA45/2017, administrative) — held administratively out of order over the 30-day filing deadline and method of filing; directly on the 42-4 timeline the overture clarifies. [minutes](../markdown/ga45_2017.md#ga45-p509)
- **[2018-06 — Edwards v. North Texas Presbytery](../cases/ga47_2019__2018-06.md)** (GA47/2019, administrative) — out of order on filing requirements expressly invoking BCO 42-4; bears on the filing-step ambiguity the overture targets. [minutes](../markdown/ga47_2019.md#ga47-p577)
- **[2024-10 — Gozé v. Hills and Plains Presbytery](../cases/ga52_2025__2024-10.md)** (GA52/2025, dismissed) — judicially out of order on timeliness of appeal under BCO 42-4, turning on what "notification" starts the 30-day clock; the most recent friction with the exact provision. [minutes](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p1011)

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
- **ga47_2019 CCB App. O II.H** (GA47/2019, not in conflict; adopted) — CCB review of Platte Valley O9 amending BCO 42-4, 43-2, 43-3 on methods/deadlines of filing judicial cases; closest CCB treatment of amending 42-4 filing mechanics. [page](../inquiries/ga47_2019__ci08.md)
- **ga47_2019 CCB App. O II.T** (GA47/2019, not in conflict; adopted) — CCB review of Philadelphia O34 amending BCO 42-4 (and 43-2/43-3/OMSJC) to clarify filing requirements and permit electronic filing; same provision and same "clarify filing" purpose. [page](../inquiries/ga47_2019__ci20.md)
- **ga49_2022 CCB App. O II.C** (GA49/2022, not in conflict; adopted) — CCB found no conflict in amending BCO 42-6 on suspension of judgment pending appeal; bears on the 42-6 leg of this overture. ⭐ [page](../inquiries/ga49_2022__ci03.md)
- **ga48_2021 CCB App. O II.N** (GA48/2021, not in conflict; adopted) — CCB review of an overture amending BCO 42-6 on the vote required to maintain a censure during appeal; same subsection. ⭐ [page](../inquiries/ga48_2021__ci14.md)
- **ga41_2013 CCB App. O II.E** (GA41/2013, in conflict) — CCB warned that adding a definitions section (proposed 42-13) could conflict with BCO 42-3 by narrowing recognized grounds of appeal; a caution relevant to any overture that "clarifies" Chapter 42 terminology. [page](../inquiries/ga41_2013__ci02.md)

### Prior overtures
- **[GA14 O37](../overtures/ga14_1986__o37.md)** (1986, Approved & ratified) — Amend BCO 42-4 and 43-2 to extend the appeal/complaint filing period to sixty days; the original substantive edit to the 42-4 deadline (later reduced to 30). [page](../markdown/ga14_1986.md#ga14-p55)
- **[GA40 O14](../overtures/ga40_2012__o14.md)** (2012, Approved & ratified) — Amend BCO 42-4 to change the start of the thirty-day filing period for appeal; closest prior successful amendment of the same sentence this overture rewrites. [page](../markdown/ga40_2012.md#ga40-p89)
- **[GA41 O5](../overtures/ga41_2013__o5.md)** (2013, Answered in the negative) — Amend BCO 42 by adding 42-13 to define terms in Chapter 42; a prior, failed "clarify Chapter 42" attempt (the CCB-conflict above attached to it). [page](../markdown/ga41_2013.md#ga41-p92)
- **[GA47 O9](../overtures/ga47_2019__o9.md)** (2019) — Amend BCO 42-4, 43-2, and 43-3 regarding method and deadlines of filing cases; same-provision filing reform. [page](../markdown/ga47_2019.md#ga47-p610)
- **[GA47 O34](../overtures/ga47_2019__o34.md)** (2021, Approved & ratified) — Amend BCO 42-4, 43-2, 43-3 and OMSJC 18-10 to allow electronic filings; the most recent ratified change to 42-4 filing mechanics. [page](../markdown/ga47_2019.md#ga47-p674)
- **[GA48 O21](../overtures/ga48_2021__o21.md)** (2021) — Amend BCO 42-6 to require a two-thirds majority for maintaining censure during appeal; directly on the 42-6 text this overture also reorders. ⭐ [page](../markdown/ga48_2021.md#ga48-p1015)
- **[GA49 O7](../overtures/ga49_2022__o7.md)** (2022) — Amend BCO 42-6 regarding suspending judgment during appeal; the 42-6 suspending-effect language is exactly what O75 re-anchors to "the filing of the written appeal." ⭐ [page](../markdown/ga49_2022.md#ga49-p1309)

### RPR exceptions
- **BCO 42-4** — 1 citation ([Savannah River](../rpr/exc/savannah-river__020.md), 48th/2021): "No record of the court's action regarding a timely filed appeal." Real-world friction over whether/when a timely appeal was acted on — the very ambiguity O75 addresses. [by provision](../index/RPR-BY-PROVISION.md)
- **BCO 42-5** — 1 citation ([Warrior](../rpr/exc/warrior__050.md), 41st/2013): "Documentation concerning appeal is not recorded in the minutes." Bears on the 42-5 Record-of-the-Case filing duty. [by provision](../index/RPR-BY-PROVISION.md)
- **BCO 42-6** — 1 citation ([Illiana](../rpr/illiana.md), 49th/2022): motion made under BCO 42-6 with no record of a continuing judicial process; touches the 42-6 suspending-effect provision. [by provision](../index/RPR-BY-PROVISION.md)

### Note
This is a chapter-level overture, so the deterministic join returned provisions=[] (no exact-provision spine); all citations above come from a topical search of the index (OVERTURES.md, cases.jsonl, INQUIRIES.md, CCB-OVERTURE-ADVICE.md, RPR-BY-PROVISION.md) plus the overture PDF, and every link/anchor was verified against the corpus. **Pruning:** roughly two dozen cases cite 42-6 only because that subsection governs suspension of judgment during any appeal (e.g., Steele 1986-4, Clark 1993-10/10b, Smith 1998-8, Plowman 2002-5, and the post-2018 deposition-appeal line — Crouse 2019-3, Dudt 2021-13, Ruff 2009-28, etc.) — these are incidental to O75, which makes only a conforming reorder of 42-6, so they are excluded; the cases kept are those that actually turn on the 42-4/42-5 *filing* step the overture rewrites. **Renumbering:** Chapter 42's subsection numbering has been stable (42-4/5/6 are long-standing), so no old-number search was needed. **Cross-links:** this overture sits on the historical 42-4 filing-reform thread (GA14 O37 → GA40 O14 → GA47 O9/O34) and the 42-6 suspension thread (GA48 O21, GA49 O7); check for any companion GA53 overture touching Chapter 43 complaint-filing, which shares 42-4's deadline mechanics. Pruned as incidental: 1997-06 Fitzsimmons v. Evangel Presbytery — the case turns on Presbytery's duty to notify appellant of the appeal hearing and to adjudicate after finding the appeal in order (BCO 42-8/42-9); the "notice" at issue is notice of the hearing, not the "notice of appeal" filing step BCO 42-4 governs; 42-4 does not appear in the case's BCO citations.

## O76 — Issue a Declaration of Thanksgiving for the USA on the 250th Anniversary
**Targets:** (statement — cites BCO 14-6.k as the enabling power) · **Source:** Calvary · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-76_Calvary_Thanksgiving.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-76_Calvary_Thanksgiving.pdf)

**What it does:** Asks the 53rd GA to issue a formal "Declaration of Thanksgiving for the United States of America on the Occasion of the 250th Anniversary of the Nation's Founding" on July 4, 2026, giving thanks to God for civil liberties (especially religious liberty) won through the War of Independence, and to spread the declaration on the minutes and publish it electronically through the AC via *byFaith*.

**Cites in its own grounds:** None. The grounds cite Scripture (Ps 136:1; 1 Tim 2:1-2), WCF 5.7 and 20.2, the 1775 Synod of New York and Philadelphia pastoral letter, the First Amendment, and BCO 14-6.k as the enabling power — but no prior PCA cases, overtures, or inquiries.

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
None found. (No SJC/CJB case construes the GA's declaratory power under BCO 14-6.k or the propriety of a commemorative thanksgiving declaration; the question is non-justiciable.)

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
None found. (BCO 14-6 inquiries in the corpus all construe *other* subsections — committee authority under 14-6/14-1, executive-session minutes under 14-6.c, involuntary dissociation under 14-6.e — none reach 14-6.k, the clause O76 invokes. Pruned as incidental; see Note.)

### Prior overtures
- **[GA3 O20](../overtures/ga03_1975__o20.md)** (1975, Adopted) — "Call for a Day of Prayer and Fasting on July 4, 1976" (Grace); the direct precedent — the PCA's own 1976 Bicentennial observance, the same July-4 / national-founding occasion O76 invokes for the Semiquincentennial. [page](../markdown/ga03_1975.md#ga03-p32)
- **[GA19 O41](../overtures/ga19_1991__o41.md)** (1991, Adopted) — "Call a Day of Thanksgiving for War Victory" (Heritage, substitute for O16); GA issuing a corporate act of thanksgiving to God tied to a national/civic event — closest in posture (thanksgiving, not lament or petition). [page](../markdown/ga19_1991.md#ga19-p59)
- **[GA14 O49](../overtures/ga14_1986__o49.md)** (1986, Adopted) — "Encourage a Day of Prayer for Those Affected by the Midwest Farm Crisis" (Siouxlands); GA calling the churches to corporate prayer over a national civic circumstance. [page](../markdown/ga14_1986.md#ga14-p47)
- **[GA35 O6](../overtures/ga35_2007__o6.md)** (2007, Adopted) — "Commemorate 500th Anniversary of Calvin's Birth" (Philadelphia Metro West, to AC); a commemorative overture marking a historical anniversary, routed to the AC for publication — closely parallel mechanism. [page](../markdown/ga35_2007.md#ga35-p576)
- **[GA35 O14](../overtures/ga35_2007__o14.md)** (2007, Adopted) — "Adopt Resolution of Praise for the Ministry of TE Paul G. Settle" (North Texas, to OC); an occasional resolution of praise/thanksgiving spread on the minutes — the same form O76 uses. [page](../markdown/ga35_2007.md#ga35-p164)
- **GA40 O37 / O44** (2012, Answered by reference / Adopted) — "Recognize 30th Anniversary of Church Unity Joining and Receiving"; anniversary-recognition declarations. [page](../markdown/ga40_2012.md#ga40-p89)
- **[GA46 O35](../overtures/ga46_2018__o35.md)** (2018, Adopted) — "Establish Subcommittee of AC to Plan PCA 50th Anniversary Celebration" (Southeast Alabama, to AC); recent anniversary-commemoration action showing current GA practice. [page](../markdown/ga46_2018.md#ga46-p77)
- **[GA50 O28](../overtures/ga50_2023__o28.md)** (2023, Approved → sent to presbyteries) — "Declare 1973 Message to All Churches a Faithful Expression of Biblical Polity Shaping the PCA" (**Calvary**, to OC, AC); the closest companion — Calvary's own prior declaration overture, same source presbytery, same OC/AC routing, declaratory form. ⭐ [page](../markdown/ga50_2023.md#ga50-p1035)

### RPR exceptions
None found. (RPR citations to BCO 14-6 are all 14-6.c executive-session-minutes exceptions — e.g., [Grace](../rpr/exc/grace__012.md) 38th/2010, [Missouri](../rpr/missouri.md) 46th/2018 — unrelated to 14-6.k; pruned as incidental.) [by provision](../index/RPR-BY-PROVISION.md)

### Note
Non-provision (statement/declaration) overture: the deterministic spine returned provisions=[], so the bearing set comes entirely from topical search. **Pruned as incidental:** the BCO 14-6 hits in inquiries (10-23 committee authority; 50-21 dissociation under 14-6.e) and RPR (executive-session minutes under 14-6.c) — none construe 14-6.k, the clause O76 actually invokes. **No judicial cases bear:** issuing a commemorative thanksgiving declaration is a legislative/declaratory act, not a justiciable one. The strongest bearing actions are the prior commemoration / day-of-thanksgiving / declaration overtures, which establish a settled GA practice of occasional civic-and-anniversary thanksgiving acts (GA3 O20 Bicentennial; GA19 O41 War Victory; GA35 O6 Calvin); the closest companion is **[GA50 O28](../overtures/ga50_2023__o28.md)**, Calvary's own 2023 declaration overture (same presbytery, same OC/AC routing). **Companion GA53 overtures (verified via ga53_join.py, same Assembly — OC will likely consolidate):** O66 (Philadelphia, "Issue a Declaration of Thanksgiving on the 250th Anniversary of the Nation's Founding"); O89 (Fellowship, "Issue a Declaration of Thanksgiving for the USA on the 250th Anniversary"); O4 (PNW, "Docket a Prayer of Thanksgiving for Adult Professions of Faith" — related genre). These three are pending same-Assembly overtures, not prior actions, so they carry no past-minutes deep-link.

## O77 — Amend RAO 4-9 so that Coordinators and the Stated Clerk are Elected to 4-year Terms
**Targets:** RAO 4-9 · **Source:** Southeast Alabama Presbytery (SEAL) · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-77_SEAL_RAO4-9.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-77_SEAL_RAO4-9.pdf)

**What it does:** Amends RAO 4-9 to replace the annual nomination/one-year election of the four Program Committee Coordinators and the Stated Clerk with election to four-year terms (deletes "annually" from both nomination clauses). Effective for the Stated Clerk at GA53 and for the four Coordinators (CDM, MNA, MTW, RUF) at GA54.

**Cites in its own grounds:** None (rationale invokes only parity with the 5-year terms of Permanent Committee members and the no-fixed-term practice of Agency heads; no prior overtures, cases, or CCB rulings cited).

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
None found.

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
- **Supplemental III.1** (GA49/2022) — Whether Committees of Commissioners may nominate substitute program coordinators; CCB ruled a CoC may only approve or disapprove a nominee, not nominate a substitute. Construes the RAO 4-9 "nominate annually a coordinator … for election" mechanism this overture rewrites. [page](../inquiries/ga49_2022__ci29.md)
- **Supplemental III.2** (GA49/2022) — Floor nomination procedure for the office of Stated Clerk; CCB advised floor nominations follow the same procedure as other contested offices and require TEC examination. Construes the RAO 4-9 Stated Clerk nomination/election clause and the TEC-examination proviso this overture preserves. [page](../inquiries/ga49_2022__ci30.md)
- **Supplemental II.2** (GA52/2025) — Floor nominations for Stated Clerk when the AC brings no nominee; CCB ruled floor nominations are permitted under RAO 3-4 even absent an AC nominee. ⭐ Recent (GA52). Construes the annual AC-nomination/election scheme for the Stated Clerk in RAO 4-9 that this overture lengthens to a four-year term. [page](../inquiries/ga52_2025__ci35.md)

### Prior overtures
- **[GA19 O43](../overtures/ga19_1991__o43.md)** (1991, Answered in the negative) — Amend RAO 4-9 to Limit Coordinators & Stated Clerk to Two Four-Year Terms (Presbytery of the Ascension). The closest prior attempt: it already proposed four-year terms for these same officers (capped at two terms) and was defeated — the precise change O77 revives, minus the cap. [page](../markdown/ga19_1991.md#ga19-p60)
- **[GA39 O2](../overtures/ga39_2011__o2.md)** (2011, Answered in the negative) — Amend RAO 4-9 to Set Term Limits for Program Committee Coordinators and Stated Clerk (South Florida Presbytery). A second prior attempt to restructure the term/length scheme of the same provision for the same offices; also defeated. [page](../markdown/ga39_2011.md#ga39-p77)

### RPR exceptions
None found.

### Note
RPR exceptions are not applicable — RAO 4-9 is a Rule of Assembly Operations, not a BCO provision subject to presbytery RPR exceptions; the spine returned rpr=[]. No renumbering applies (not in bco_renumberings.jsonl). **GA53 RAO 4-9 cluster — cross-link O40, O41, O43, O73, O77:** O77 is functionally identical to **O43 (PNW)**, which likewise moves Coordinators to four-year terms (O77 adds the Stated Clerk and an effective-date scheme); O40 (Savannah River) sets calendar-year terms; O41 (Savannah River) and O73 (TE Hooper) instead keep annual election but raise the vote threshold to 2/3. The two prior overtures (GA19 O43, GA39 O2) are the highest-value bearing actions: both proposed amending the very same term structure of RAO 4-9 and both were answered in the negative, signaling repeated past resistance. The three inquiries are provision-exact hits retained (none pruned as incidental) because each construes the RAO 4-9 nomination/election clauses that O77 rewrites; they are procedural-mechanism rulings rather than rulings on term length, which is the only sense in which their bearing is partial.

## O78 — Amend RAO 4-21 to Authorize Electronic Meetings for GA Committees and Commissions
**Targets:** RAO 4-21 (new), existing 4-21 renumbered → 4-22, conform cross-ref in RAO 14-11.a · **Source:** Southeast Alabama Presbytery (SEAL) · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-78_SEAL_RAO4-21.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-78_SEAL_RAO4-21.pdf)

**What it does:** Inserts a new RAO 4-21 authorizing GA committees and commissions established by the BCO and RAO — except the Overtures Committee and Committees of Commissioners — to meet electronically (RONR 12th ed. 9:30-36) if they so provide in their own rules, and expressly authorizes ad hoc/ad interim committees to meet electronically at the call of the Chairman/Convenor; the existing 4-21 (Guidelines for Keeping Minutes) is renumbered 4-22. Purpose: regularize a practice many committees already follow by custom but which RONR 9:35 requires be expressly authorized by the appointing assembly.

**Cites in its own grounds:** No prior overtures, SJC cases, or CCB rulings by id. Its rationale cites BCO 12-6 (Sessions may meet electronically) and BCO 13-4 (Presbyteries may meet electronically) as "recently amended," OMSJC 4.1 (SJC may meet by telephone conference), and RONR (12th ed.) 9:30-36, 9:35, 2:8, 2:25.

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
None found.

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
- **17-82 III, 8** (GA17/1989, advice given) — CCB construed BCO 13-4 (the Presbytery analogue O78 invokes) and ruled **telephone conference meetings are impermissible** absent authorization; the historical baseline the recent BCO 12-6/13-4 amendments reversed and that O78 now extends to GA committees — directly bears on the requirement that electronic meetings be expressly authorized rather than left to custom. [page](../inquiries/ga17_1989__ci02.md)
- **27-43 II.2** (GA27/1999, advice given) — CCB advised a presbytery may receive a candidate via "interactive electronic means" to satisfy BCO 18-3's appearance requirement; an early recognition of electronic participation's legitimacy in church courts, supporting the overture's claim that the Church's framework already accepts electronic meetings. [page](../inquiries/ga27_1999__ci02.md)
- **II.D** (GA50/2023, not in conflict; Adopted 8-0-0) — CCB found Southern New England's overture amending RAO 4-21.d (Committees of Commissioners reviewing compliance) not in conflict; bears as a prior amendment to the same RAO 4-21 paragraph O78 renumbers to 4-22. [page](../inquiries/ga50_2023__ci04.md)
- **II.I** (GA51/2024, not in conflict; Adopted 8-0-0) — CCB found the overture amending RAO 4-21.d (enrollment-data reporting from higher-ed institutions) not in conflict; another recent amendment to the same paragraph being renumbered. [page](../inquiries/ga51_2024__ci09.md)

### Prior overtures
- **[GA50 O7](../overtures/ga50_2023__o7.md)** (2023, Adopted final) — Amend RAO 4-21.d to Require Committees to Record GA Instruction Compliance in Minutes (Southern New England); a prior successful amendment to the same RAO 4-21 minutes-guidelines paragraph O78 renumbers to 4-22. ⭐ [page](../markdown/ga50_2023.md#ga50-p979)
- **[GA51 O14](../overtures/ga51_2024__o14.md)** (2024, Adopted final) — Amend RAO 4-21.d to Require Enrollment Data from Higher Education Institutions (Northwest Georgia); another recent amendment to the same paragraph. ⭐ [page](../markdown/ga51_2024.md#ga51-p1270)
- **[GA51 O32](../overtures/ga51_2024__o32.md)** (2024, Carried over) — From Eastern Pennsylvania, matched as an RAO 4-21 amendment; carried over with no final outcome, bears as a pending edit to the same paragraph. ⭐ [page](../markdown/ga51_2024.md#ga51-p1272)

### RPR exceptions
None found.

### Note
**Companion to O79** (Calvary Presbytery) — verbatim same title and target (new RAO 4-21 on electronic meetings); the Overtures Committee will consolidate the two, so they should be tracked together. The exact-provision spine matches the string "RAO 4-21" broadly, but O78 inserts a NEW 4-21 and pushes the existing 4-21 (minutes guidelines) to 4-22 — so the spine's genuinely bearing hits are those touching the paragraph being renumbered (RAO 4-21.d: GA50 O7 / II.D, GA51 O14 / II.I, kept above). PRUNED as incidental: GA47 II.G/II.J/II.O/II.P/II.R (the non-ordained-persons cluster citing RAO 4-21.c.6 in passing) and GA47 III.A (SJC-eligibility, a 20-provision list that merely includes RAO 4-21) — none construes electronic-meeting authority or the renumbered provision. The two highest-value bearing actions (GA17 17-82 III,8 and GA27 27-43 II.2) are TOPICAL supplements the provision-exact spine missed, found by concept search on electronic/telephone meetings. The BCO 12-6 / 13-4 electronic-meeting amendments the overture cites in its rationale do not appear as cleanly-titled rows in the OVERTURES index, so no deep-link is asserted for them.

## O79 — Amend RAO 4-21 to Authorize Electronic Meetings for GA Committees and Commissions
**Targets:** RAO 4-21 (new; existing 4-21 renumbered → 4-22; conform cross-ref RAO 14-11.a) · **Source:** Calvary Presbytery · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-79_Calvary_RAO4-21.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-79_Calvary_RAO4-21.pdf)

**What it does:** Inserts a new RAO 4-21 expressly authorizing General Assembly committees and commissions (except the Overtures Committee, Nominating Committee, and Committees of Commissioners) to meet electronically for called meetings under their own rules, and directly authorizing ad hoc/ad interim committees to meet electronically at the call of the Chairman or Convener; the existing 4-21 (minutes guidelines) is renumbered 4-22, with a conforming cross-reference fix in RAO 14-11.a.

**Cites in its own grounds:** RONR (12th ed.) 9:30–36, 9:35, 2:8, 2:25; BCO 12-6 (electronic Session meetings); BCO 13-4 (electronic Presbytery meetings); OMSJC 4.1 (SJC telephone conference) — cited as constitutional/parliamentary precedent, not as prior overtures/cases/inquiries by number.

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
None found.

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
- **17-82 III, 8** (GA17/1989, advice given) — CCB construed BCO 13-4 (the Presbytery analogue O79 invokes) and ruled **telephone conference meetings are impermissible** absent express authorization; the historical baseline the recent BCO 12-6/13-4 amendments reversed and that O79 now extends to GA committees — directly bears on the requirement that electronic meetings be expressly authorized rather than left to custom. [page](../inquiries/ga17_1989__ci02.md)
- **27-43 II.2** (GA27/1999, advice given) — CCB advised a presbytery may receive a candidate via "interactive electronic means" to satisfy BCO 18-3's appearance requirement; an early recognition of electronic participation's legitimacy in church courts, supporting the overture's claim that the Church's framework already accepts electronic meetings. [page](../inquiries/ga27_1999__ci02.md)
- **GA50 CCB II.D** (GA50/2023, not in conflict; adopted 8-0-0) — found Southern New England's overture expanding RAO 4-21.d (Committees of Commissioners reviewing compliance policies) not in conflict; construes the same paragraph this overture renumbers. [page](../inquiries/ga50_2023__ci04.md)
- **GA51 CCB II.I** (GA51/2024, not in conflict; adopted 8-0-0) — found Northwest Georgia's overture amending RAO 4-21.d (enrollment-data reporting) not in conflict; the most recent CCB construction of RAO 4-21, showing the section is live and routinely amendable. [page](../inquiries/ga51_2024__ci09.md)

### Prior overtures
- **[GA50 O7](../overtures/ga50_2023__o7.md)** (2023, Adopted (final)) — Amend RAO 4-21.d to require committees to record GA-instruction compliance in minutes; recent successful amendment to the very paragraph this overture renumbers. ⭐ [page](../markdown/ga50_2023.md#ga50-p979)
- **[GA51 O14](../overtures/ga51_2024__o14.md)** (2024, Adopted (final)) — Amend RAO 4-21.d to require enrollment data from higher-education institutions; recent successful RAO 4-21 amendment. ⭐ [page](../markdown/ga51_2024.md#ga51-p1270)
- **[GA51 O32](../overtures/ga51_2024__o32.md)** (2024, Carried over) — Eastern Pennsylvania RAO 4-21.d-related overture, carried over; a pending recent attempt touching the same paragraph. ⭐ [page](../markdown/ga51_2024.md#ga51-p1272)

### RPR exceptions
None found.

### Note
Companion/duplicate: **O78** (Southeast Alabama / SEAL Presbytery) has the identical title and the same RAO 4-21 target — O78 and O79 should be considered together by the Overtures Committee. This overture's question (electronic meetings) is novel for RAO 4: the exact-provision spine returns no judicial cases and no RPR. The two highest-value bearing actions (GA17 17-82 III,8 and GA27 27-43 II.2) are topical supplements the provision-exact spine missed, found by concept search on electronic/telephone meetings; they are included above. The BCO 12-6 / 13-4 electronic-meeting amendments the overture cites in its rationale do not appear as cleanly-titled rows in the OVERTURES index, so no deep-link is asserted for them. PRUNED as incidental: GA47 CCB inquiry III.A (SJC/agency-board eligibility — cites RAO 4-21 only inside a long RAO 4 list) and the GA47 CCB cluster II.G / II.J / II.O / II.P / II.R (non-ordained persons on GA committees, all citing RAO 4-21.c.6 on committee composition) — these construe membership/composition, not electronic meetings, and do not bear on this change. The kept inquiries and prior overtures all concern RAO 4-21.d; they bear because (a) they confirm RAO 4-21 is a live, frequently-amended rule, and (b) this overture renumbers the existing 4-21 to 4-22, so the renumbering mechanics must not break the 4-21.d cross-references those recent amendments created.

## O80 — Erect Ad Interim Committee on Critical Theory and Critical Race Theory
**Targets:** (committee — no BCO provision; erect AIC under RAO 9-1) · **Source:** Calvary · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-80_Calvary_CRT.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-80_Calvary_CRT.pdf)

**What it does:** Asks GA53 to erect and convene a new Ad Interim Study Committee (RAO 9-1) to study Critical Race Theory from a Reformed exegetical, confessional, and theological perspective — assessing whether CRT conforms to Scripture and the Westminster Standards — and to give the Assembly pastoral guidance on addressing CRT; moderator-appointed, budget $10,000/year from designated AC gifts.

**Cites in its own grounds:** GA52 (2025) Christian Nationalism study committee (cited as the right-wing counterpart this CRT study would "compare and contrast"); GA52 (2025) overture directing the Stated Clerk not to collect ethnicity statistics — noted as answered in the affirmative (Overtures Cmte 76-28-3; floor 1184-361). No prior judicial cases or constitutional inquiries cited.

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
None found. (See Note — the only race-adjacent SJC cases in the corpus, 2008-18 and 2009-02, are pruned as incidental.)

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
None found.

### Prior overtures
- **[GA48 O47](../overtures/ga48_2021__o47.md)** (2021, Answered in the negative) — "Form Study Committee to Examine Critical Race Theory" (Chesapeake). The closest prior attempt: the same denomination-level request to study CRT, declined by GA48. ⭐ [p.1115](../markdown/ga48_2021.md#ga48-p1098), [p.1149](../markdown/ga48_2021.md#ga48-p1132)
- **[GA48 O36](../overtures/ga48_2021__o36.md)** (2021, Answered in the negative) — "Appoint Ad Interim Study Committee on White Supremacy" (Chesapeake). A companion 2021 attempt to erect a race-ideology study committee, also declined. ⭐ [p.1085](../markdown/ga48_2021.md#ga48-p1068), [p.1148](../markdown/ga48_2021.md#ga48-p1131)
- **[GA49 O41](../overtures/ga49_2022__o41.md)** (2022, Other) — "Declare Critical Race Theory Inconsistent with Biblical and Reformed Theology" (Session of Bethel Christian Church-Chicago). Sought a GA declaration on CRT's theological status — the substantive conclusion O80 would have a committee study and report on. ⭐ [p.1398](../markdown/ga49_2022.md#ga49-p1381), [p.1426](../markdown/ga49_2022.md#ga49-p1409)
- **[GA50 O18](../overtures/ga50_2023__o18.md)** (2023, Answered in the negative) — "Affirm Christ-Centered Racial Reconciliation and Reject Critical Theory Ideology" (multiple Sessions). Directly on the same CRT/critical-theory question; GA declined to make the statement. ⭐ [p.1015](../markdown/ga50_2023.md#ga50-p1007), [p.1084](../markdown/ga50_2023.md#ga50-p1076)
- **[GA52 O47](../overtures/ga52_2025__o47.md)** (2025, Adopted (final)) — "Erect an Ad Interim Study Committee on Christian Nationalism" (Great Lakes). The successful companion study committee O80 expressly invokes as the left/right counterpart; live precedent for erecting an ideology study committee. ⭐ [p.1300](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p1298), [p.1363](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p1361)
- **[GA52 O3](../overtures/ga52_2025__o3.md)** (2025, Answered by reference) — "Erect Ad Interim Study Committee on Christian Nationalism" (Arizona). One of the Christian Nationalism requests answered by reference to O47; shows how parallel study-committee overtures were consolidated. ⭐ [p.1169](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p1167), [p.1359](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p1357)
- **[GA52 O42](../overtures/ga52_2025__o42.md)** (2025, Adopted (final)) — "Direct the Stated Clerk Not to Collect Statistical Data on Age or Ethnicity" (Calvary). The very action O80's grounds cite (same presbytery); evidences the ongoing PCA debate over race/ethnicity O80 says warrants study. ⭐ [p.1289](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p1287), [p.1363](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p1361)
- **[GA52 O43](../overtures/ga52_2025__o43.md)** (2025, Adopted (final)) — "Amend RAO 4-11 to Prohibit Collection of Member Age and Ethnicity Data" (Calvary). Companion to O42; the RAO change that enacted the ethnicity-data position O80 cites. ⭐ [p.1291](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p1289), [p.1363](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p1361)
- **[GA44 O45](../overtures/ga44_2016__o45.md)** (2016, Adopted (final)) — "Form a Racial and Ethnic Reconciliation Study Committee" (Potomac). Precedent that GA will erect a study committee on race; produced the reconciliation report the CRT debate later contested. [p.651](../markdown/ga44_2016.md#ga44-p649), [p.744](../markdown/ga44_2016.md#ga44-p742)
- **[GA44 O4](../overtures/ga44_2016__o4.md)** (2016, Answered by reference) — "Adopt Steps Toward Racial Reconciliation" / Overture 4 on Racial Reconciliation (Heartland, lead overture of the 2016 cluster). Foundational racial-reconciliation action whose interpretation CRT critics dispute. [p.572](../markdown/ga44_2016.md#ga44-p570), [p.741](../markdown/ga44_2016.md#ga44-p739)
- **[GA32 O20](../overtures/ga32_2004__o20.md)** (2004, Adopted (final)) — "Adopt Statement of Repentance and Commitment to Racial Reconciliation" (Nashville). Earliest PCA standing statement on race; part of the body of action O80 would study alongside CRT. [p.455](../markdown/ga32_2004.md#ga32-p453)
- **[GA30 O20](../overtures/ga30_2002__o20.md)** (2002, Adopted (final)) — "Adopt Statement on Racial Reconciliation" (Nashville). The denomination's first racial-reconciliation statement; background for O80's racial-unity grounds. [p.78](../markdown/ga30_2002.md#ga30-p76), [p.267](../markdown/ga30_2002.md#ga30-p265)

### RPR exceptions
None found. (O80 amends no BCO provision, so no Record of the Proceedings of Review / RPR exceptions attach.)

### Note
O80 is a committee-erection overture with no BCO target, so the deterministic provision-join returned no spine hits; all bearing actions were found by concept search in /workspace/index (OVERTURES.md). It is a near-verbatim re-run of **[GA48 O47](../overtures/ga48_2021__o47.md)** (Form Study Committee to Examine CRT, declined 2021) and shares ground with GA48 O36 (White Supremacy), GA49 O41 (declare CRT inconsistent), and GA50 O18 (reject critical-theory ideology) — every prior CRT/critical-theory request has been declined or "answered" without a committee, even as parallel ideology committees succeeded (GA44 O45 racial reconciliation; GA52 O47 Christian Nationalism, which O80 cites as its counterweight). Cross-link the GA53 Christian Nationalism companion overture (**O90**, append Reformed Christian Politics to the Christian Nationalism AIC report) noted in the first pass. **Pruned as incidental:** SJC cases 2008-18 (Hutchinson & Bulkeley v. Western Carolina) and 2009-02 (Morton Smith v. Western Carolina) — both concern an RE's published views on "race and IQ" and turn purely on discipline/due-process (BCO 38-1, 24-6.4), not on whether GA should study CRT; they do not bear on the committee question. No constitutional inquiries or CCB advice address CRT or study-committee erection. No renumbering caveat applies (no provision targeted).

## O81 — Amend RAO 1-1 to Require Serving Wine and Grape Juice for the Lord's Supper at GA
**Targets:** RAO 1-1 · **Source:** Potomac · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-81_Potomac_RAO1-1.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-81_Potomac_RAO1-1.pdf)

**What it does:** Amends RAO 1-1 (the order for the GA opening worship service) by adding a sentence requiring that, in the administration of the Lord's Supper at General Assembly, both wine and grape juice "shall be provided and clearly identified, to respect the consciences of all commissioners," and directs the Stated Clerk to implement it beginning with the next GA.

**Cites in its own grounds:** None — it cites only Scripture (Matt. 26:29, Ps. 104:15, Isa. 25:6), WCF 29.3, and WLC Q.168–169; no prior PCA cases, overtures, or inquiries by number.

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
None found.

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
- **29-28 III.5** (GA29/2001) — CCB advised Great Lakes Presbytery that BCO 58-4 "allows no exception of practice in administering the Lord's Supper." Bears on how far a court may regulate the manner/elements of the Supper, which is the question O81 raises by mandating provision of both elements at GA. [page](../inquiries/ga29_2001__ci05.md)
- **21-56 III** (GA21/1993) — GA construed the permissible scope of communion practice under BCO 58-4 (denied closed communion; affirmed open/close communion). Background on the Assembly's prior treatment of regulating practice at the Table. [page](../inquiries/ga21_1993__ci01.md)

### Prior overtures
- **[GA18 O14](../overtures/ga18_1990__o14.md)** (1990, Answered in the negative) — Southwest's overture to amend BCO 58-5 by replacing "Wine" with "Fruit of the Vine" — the most directly on-point prior attempt to legislate the communion element. GA declined to alter the element language, leaving wine/grape-juice practice unregulated; O81 instead mandates providing both at GA. [page](../markdown/ga18_1990.md#ga18-p72)
- **[GA52 O12](../overtures/ga52_2025__o12.md)** (2025, Approved but not ratified) — Providence's overture to amend BCO 58-5 on distribution of the Lord's Supper; the most recent live amendment activity around how the Supper is administered. ⭐ [page](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p1189)
- **[GA21 O25](../overtures/ga21_1993__o25.md)** (1993, Answered in the negative) — Third RPC's overture to change the invitation to the Sacrament of the Lord's Supper; another attempt to regulate Supper practice that GA declined. [page](../markdown/ga21_1993.md#ga21-p55)

### RPR exceptions
None found.

### Note
The deterministic spine (RAO 1-1, exact provision) returned only two CCB-advice hits — II.Q (GA48, telecommunication meetings) and II.Y (GA49, virtual meeting protocol). Both are PRUNED as incidental: they cite RAO 1-1 only because it governs the GA opening session and concern nothing about the Lord's Supper or its elements. The genuinely bearing actions are topical (the elements/practice of the Supper under BCO 58-4/58-5), found via concept search of the index — none surfaced in the exact-provision join because O81 places its new rule in RAO 1-1 rather than BCO 58-5. No renumbering of RAO 1-1 was found. The closest precedent is GA18 O14 (wine vs. "fruit of the vine"), which shows GA's longstanding reluctance to legislate the communion element; O81 sidesteps that by requiring availability of both rather than prescribing one.
