## O82 — Amend BCO 12, 13, and 25 re Right of Congregation to Consent to those who Exercise Authority
**Targets:** BCO 12, 13, 25 (12-1, 13-9, 25-2) · **Source:** Rocky Mountain Presbytery · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-82_RMP_1213.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-82_RMP_1213.pdf)

**What it does:** Amends BCO 13-9 so a Presbytery may assume original jurisdiction over a church "with the consent of the Session or the congregation" (and adds "with their consent" qualifiers throughout 13-9.f–g), and amends BCO 12-1 and 25-2 to create a constitutional mechanism by which a lone ruling elder (or the Presbytery, via new 13-9.i) may convene a congregational meeting of an elder-less/sessionless church to obtain its consent to appoint a temporary government under BCO 15-1 and 16-2. The stated aim is to bar a Presbytery from imposing a commission as an interim Session over a congregation without its consent.

**Cites in its own grounds:** Judicial Case #5, 13th GA (Preg v. Missouri Presbytery, 1985, on 13-9/11-4); SJC Case 90-4 (Chappell v. Eastern Carolina Presbytery, 19th GA, 1991); SJC Case 2001-8 (Lee v. Korean Capital Presbytery, 30th GA, 2002, citing BCO 25-11); SJC Case 2001-34 (Nichols & Couch v. James River Presbytery, 33rd GA, 2005). Also quotes Preliminary Principles 6 & 7, BCO 3-1, 3-4, 11-1/11-2, 16-2, 25-8/9/10/11, Morton Smith's Commentary, and Williamson & Cannada's Historic Polity of the PCA.

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
- **[5 — TE S. Michael Preg, Jr., et al. v. Missouri Presbytery](../cases/ga13_1985__case1.md)** (13th GA/1985, sustained 16-0) — The Judicial Case #5 the overture quotes verbatim: the Commission held BCO 13-9 "contains no express provision … as would permit a presbytery to require" a visit "without a request by or a specific problem in the session or congregation," and warned against higher-court encroachment on lower courts. Directly construes the 13-9 power O82 narrows with "with their consent." [minutes](../markdown/ga13_1985.md#ga13-p128)
- **[1990-04 — Charles E. Chappell v. Eastern Carolina Presbytery](../cases/ga19_1991__1990-04.md)** (19th GA/1991, sustained) — The "SJC Case 90-4" the overture relies on: Presbytery determined a Session could not exercise its authority and assumed original jurisdiction by appointing a temporary Session over the church; SJC held the Presbytery erred, that presbyteries may not assume jurisdiction and act over a church without the congregation's consent. The precise scenario O82's 13-9 amendment codifies. [minutes](../markdown/ga19_1991.md#ga19-p488)
- **[2001-08 — TE Andy Lee v. Korean Capital Presbytery](../cases/ga30_2002__2001-08.md)** (30th GA/2002, sustained) — The "Case 2001-8" the overture quotes: SJC held a Presbytery erred in suspending a Session and appointing a commission to act for it, citing BCO 25-11 that congregational rights may never be taken away "without the express consent and affirmative action" of the congregation. Direct support for the consent requirement O82 writes into 13-9. [minutes](../markdown/ga30_2002.md#ga30-p133)
- **[2001-34 — RE Leland Nichols & RE Sam Couch v. James River Presbytery](../cases/ga33_2005__2001-34_2002-02_2002-03.md)** (33rd GA/2005, sustained in part) — The "SJC 2001-34" the overture quotes for the "act on / act for / act against" framework: a higher court may not "act for" a lower court and may not force civil action against a congregation without a congregational vote. Frames the non-hierarchical principle O82 codifies. [minutes](../markdown/ga33_2005.md#ga33-p72)

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
- **CCB advice, App. O II.E (CI ga39_2011)** (39th GA/2011) — On the very gap O82 fixes: the CCB reviewed a proposed overture on temporary governance for elder-less churches and warned it may conflict with Preliminary Principles 2 & 6 and BCO 12-1 if read as prescriptive. Most direct prior CCB treatment of the 12-1 temporary-government mechanism. [page](../inquiries/ga39_2011__ci01.md)
- **CI #15 (CCB ga14_1986)** (14th GA/1986) — Advised that a congregation cannot dissolve its Session, but the Presbytery may assume jurisdiction under BCO 13-9; construes the same 13-9 original-jurisdiction power O82 conditions on consent. [page](../inquiries/ga14_1986__ci18.md)
- **13-45 III, 65 (CCB ga13_1985)** (13th GA/1985) — Advised that BCO 13-9 grants Presbytery the prerogative to initiate regular visitation of its churches; the same-year counterpart to Judicial Case #5, and the very "visit … for the purpose of inquiring into and redressing the evils" clause O82 amends to add "with their consent." [page](../inquiries/ga13_1985__ci05.md)
- **II.F (CCB ga49_2022)** (49th GA/2022) — CCB found no conflict in amending BCO 25-2 to add a threshold for calling congregational meetings; bears on the 25-2 congregational-meeting machinery O82 also amends. [page](../inquiries/ga49_2022__ci06.md)
- **II.H (CCB ga51_2024)** (51st GA/2024) — CCB found a recent overture to amend BCO 13-9 (adding presbytery TE-care duties) not in conflict; recent CCB treatment of amending the same section. [page](../inquiries/ga51_2024__ci08.md)

### Prior overtures
- **[GA39 O10](../overtures/ga39_2011__o10.md)** (2011, Approved but not ratified) — "Amend BCO 12 to Provide Temporary Governance for Churches Without Ruling Elders." The closest prior attempt at the same change O82 makes; passed the floor but failed ratification, leaving the gap O82 now targets. [page](../markdown/ga39_2011.md#ga39-p78)
- **[GA27 O10](../overtures/ga27_1999__o10.md)** (1999, Adopted/final) — "Amend BCO to Authorize Interim Sessions." Created the interim-Session mechanism (BCO 15-1) that O82 presupposes and builds a consent-procedure around. [page](../markdown/ga27_1999.md#ga27-p50)
- **[GA35 O10](../overtures/ga35_2007__o10.md)** (2007, Approved & ratified 2008) — "Amend BCO 12-1 and 12-2 to Revise Session Quorum Requirements." Amended the same 12-1 quorum sentence O82 edits; shows the section's drafting history. [page](../markdown/ga35_2007.md#ga35-p160)
- **[GA49 O11](../overtures/ga49_2022__o11.md)** (2022, Answered in the negative) — "Amend BCO 25-2.e and Add BCO 25-2.f Regarding Threshold for Large Church Congregational Meetings." ⭐ A recent attempt to amend the same 25-2 congregational-meeting provision. [page](../markdown/ga49_2022.md#ga49-p1299)
- **[GA51 O10](../overtures/ga51_2024__o10.md)** (2024, Answered in the negative) — "Add Presbytery TE Care to BCO 13-9." ⭐ The most recent attempt to amend BCO 13-9; bears on the appetite for and drafting of 13-9 changes. [page](../markdown/ga51_2024.md#ga51-p1270)

### RPR exceptions
- **BCO 13-9 (with 3-1, 16-1, 25-8–11)** — [Potomac](../rpr/exc/potomac__009.md) Presbytery, 39th GA (2011): exception raised that the "Presbytery appointed a commission to act as the interim session" — the exact real-world friction O82 addresses (a Presbytery imposing an interim Session over a church). [by provision](../index/RPR-BY-PROVISION.md)
- **BCO 12-1 / 25-2** — Only 2 BCO 12-1 RPR citations and the 25-2 cites are unrelated; the bulk of the 33 BCO 13-9 RPR exceptions concern failure to review session records (13-9.b), which is incidental to this overture and is pruned. [by provision](../index/RPR-BY-PROVISION.md)

### Note
Provision-exact spine returned provisions=[] (chapter-level overture), so all citations come from topical search of /workspace/index and from the overture's own grounds; no renumbering affects chapters 12, 13, or 25. PRUNED as incidental: the large family of "assume original jurisdiction" overtures under BCO 33-1/34-1 (GA29 O9/O11, GA30 O5/O18/O30, GA37 O3, GA40 O18, GA41 O16, GA49 O8/O9, GA50 O21, GA52 O7) — these concern a higher court assuming jurisdiction over individual members/ministers in *discipline*, a distinct mechanism from the 13-9 Presbytery-over-Session/congregation jurisdiction O82 addresses; the per-church "Assume Original Jurisdiction re TE Greg Johnson/Leithart" overtures are case-specific and do not bear. Also pruned: 13-9.f dissolution/dismissal overtures (GA12 O32, GA23 O3/O6, GA24 O28) and the 13-9.b sessional-records RPR exceptions, which touch the section but not this question. Judgment call: SJC 90-4 = Chappell (1990-04) per corpus, the lead Eastern Carolina case the overture cites to M19GA pp.488–508. Pruned as incidental: 1990-08 Bowen v. Eastern Carolina Presbytery — the case's actual holdings are (a) BCO 43-10 does not permit a higher court to annul completed ordinations after the fact, and (b) infant baptism and limited atonement are fundamentals of the system of doctrine; the 13-9 citation is incidental (same passage quoted from Chappell); the case does not construe the consent-to-jurisdiction question O82 addresses.

---

## O83 — Require Courses on Scripture and Doctrine at Covenant College and Covenant Seminary Be Taught by Ordained Elders
**Targets:** (institutions — no BCO amendment; grounds invoke BCO 7-2, 8-1, 8-5, 21-4, 12-5, 21-5, 24-1) · **Source:** Northwest Georgia Presbytery (to CC, CTS) · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-83_NWGA_BibleInstructors.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-83_NWGA_BibleInstructors.pdf)

**What it does:** Asks the Assembly to affirm that courses systematically teaching the Bible or Christian doctrine at Covenant College or Covenant Seminary should be taught only by men examined and ordained as teaching or ruling elders in NAPARC denominations, and to direct both Agencies to amend their bylaws to enforce this. It rests on the prohibition of women teaching or exercising authority over men (1 Tim. 2:12–13) read as a binding creation ordinance reaching beyond gathered worship.

**Cites in its own grounds:** No prior GA cases, overtures, or inquiries cited by number — only Scripture and BCO provisions (7-2; 8-1; 8-5; 21-4; 12-5; 21-5; 24-1).

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
- **[Case 99-1 — The John Wood Matter (Investigative Report)](../markdown/ga29_2001.md#ga29-p70)** (GA29/2001, other — no strong presumption of guilt; process declined) — The single judicial action squarely on the question O83 presses: whether a woman teaching/speaking authoritatively (Dr. Linda Eure at Cedar Springs' evening worship) and a TE's views favoring women preaching fall outside the Standards. The SJC declined process, finding "no clear evidence that TE Wood's views are outside the bounds of our Standards" — i.e., the Assembly's courts have not treated the 1 Tim. 2:12 boundary as settled in the maximal direction O83 assumes. [minutes](../markdown/ga29_2001.md#ga29-p70)

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
- **GA47 CCB II.B** (GA47/2019) — On Northwest Georgia Presbytery's own Overture 2 to release CTS from Assembly oversight, the CCB found the overture "creates a conflict with the RAO and Corporate By-Laws." Directly bearing: O83 (same presbytery, same institutions) likewise directs the Agencies to amend their bylaws, and the same RAO/Bylaws-governance objection is likely to recur. [page](../inquiries/ga47_2019__ci02.md)
- **GA50 CCB II.K** (GA50/2023) — On Bryce Avenue's Overture 15, the CCB found that amending BCO 53 to disallow women from exhorting/preaching/teaching in corporate worship is "not in conflict with the BCO." Bears as the closest recent CCB reading of the women-teaching boundary; note it concerns *worship* (BCO 53), whereas O83 reaches into *academic* instruction outside worship. [page](../inquiries/ga50_2023__ci11.md)

### Prior overtures
- **[GA51 O29](../overtures/ga51_2024__o29.md)** (2024, Answered by reference) — Bryce Avenue's "Amend BCO 53 to Prohibit Women from Preaching in Chapel and Campus Ministry Services," targeting chapel and campus-ministry settings. ⭐ Closest precedent for extending the male-only teaching rule into educational/campus contexts. [page](../markdown/ga51_2024.md#ga51-p1182)
- **[GA50 O15](../overtures/ga50_2023__o15.md)** (2023, Referred) — Bryce Avenue's "Amend BCO 53 to Disallow Women from Preaching or Teaching in Worship." ⭐ Same campaign as GA51 O29; grounds parallel O83's (creation ordinance, 1 Tim. 2). [page](../markdown/ga50_2023.md#ga50-p1002)
- **[GA47 O2](../overtures/ga47_2019__o2.md)** (2019, Answered in the negative) — Northwest Georgia Presbytery, "Encourage Covenant Theological Seminary Toward Release from Assembly Oversight." Same presbytery, same institution (CTS); NWGA's prior, unsuccessful attempt to legislate CTS governance, drawing the CCB conflict noted above. [page](../markdown/ga47_2019.md#ga47-p584)
- **[GA38 O25](../overtures/ga38_2010__o25.md)** (2010, Answered in the negative) — Northwest Georgia Presbytery, "Reaffirm BCO Standards on Roles of Men and Women in Church Office," asserting the BCO sufficiently fixes the male-only ordained roles. Same presbytery, same theological premise as O83's grounds. [page](../markdown/ga38_2010.md#ga38-p394)
- **[GA29 O25](../overtures/ga29_2001__o25.md)** (2001, Answered in the negative) — Grace Presbytery, "Forbid Women to Preach or Teach in Corporate Worship," with whereas clauses nearly identical to O83 ("a woman shall not teach or exercise authority over a man… result of the creation ordinance"). CCB ruled it "touches on issues not properly before the Committee since it does not seek constitutional amendment or constitutional advice" — a procedural warning that bears directly on O83, which likewise seeks an affirmation/directive rather than a BCO amendment. [page](../markdown/ga29_2001.md#ga29-p222)
- **[GA27 O16](../overtures/ga27_1999__o16.md)** (1999, Answered in the negative) — Western Carolina Presbytery, "Forbid Women to Preach/Teach at Worship Services." Earliest of the recurring "forbid women to teach" overtures, all answered in the negative. [page](../markdown/ga27_1999.md#ga27-p172)
- **[GA46 O26](../overtures/ga46_2018__o26.md)** (2018, approved → presbyteries; ratification not located) — Tennessee Valley Presbytery, "Amend BCO 14-1.11 to Allow Non-ordained Trustees of Covenant College." Bears as a counter-current: the Assembly recently moved to *loosen* ordination requirements around Covenant College governance — the opposite direction from O83. [page](../markdown/ga46_2018.md#ga46-p722)

### RPR exceptions
None found. (O83 amends no BCO provision, and RPR reviews presbytery records, not agency/college bylaws — so no presbytery-record exception attaches to this subject.)

### Note
Provision-exact spine returned provisions=[] (institutional/resolution overture directing Agency bylaws, not a BCO amendment), so this page is built entirely from topical search of the index — the prior pass wrongly reported "no SJC/CCB precedent." PRUNING: the join surfaced no cases for any provision; the BCO chapters named only in O83's *grounds* (7, 8, 12, 21, 24) are cited in passing by many unrelated discipline cases (e.g., John Wood itself cites 7-2, 12-5, 21-5), but only John Wood actually construes the women-teaching question, so all other incidental provision hits are pruned. JUDGMENT CALLS: (1) the GA29/GA50/GA51 line concerns women in *worship* (BCO 53), while O83 uniquely reaches into *academic* instruction at the agencies — a novel extension, so those bear by analogy, not on all fours; (2) the GA47 O2 and GA46 O26 Covenant-College/CTS-governance items bear on the *mechanism* (directing agencies to amend bylaws / ordination status of those serving the institutions) rather than the women-teaching premise. No renumbering caveat: O83 cites current BCO numbering and amends nothing. No companion GA53 overture on this exact subject was found in the join.

---

## O84 — Amend BCO 12 and 13 to Require Annual Attestation of Officer's Views
**Targets:** BCO 12, 13 · **Source:** NWGA (Northwest Georgia Presbytery) · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-84_NWGA_1213.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-84_NWGA_1213.pdf)

**What it does:** Adds BCO 12-5.g / 12-6 and 13-9.h / 13-10 (renumbering the following paragraphs) to make it a power of the Session and Presbytery "to maintain sound doctrine," and requires each court to *annually record an attestation* from every officer (RE/deacon; TE/licentiate) stating whether his views remain unchanged or, if changed, in what regard he is now dubious or in disagreement with the Confession or Catechisms — recorded in his own words with the court's judgment, per the RAO 16-3.e.7 categories.

**Cites in its own grounds:** No prior cases, overtures, or inquiries. Cites RAO 16-3 (Good Faith Subscription), BCO 24-6 (minister's ethical burden to disclose a change of views), and Scripture (Jude 3; 1 Tim. 4:15-16).

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
- **[2020-05 — Speck v. Missouri Presbytery](../cases/ga49_2022__2020-05.md)** (GA49/2022, sustained) — Sets the standard a court must apply when examining whether a TE's views accord with the Standards (BCO 11-3, 11-4, 13-9(f), not the 34-5 "vitals" test); directly bears on what a court's "judgment" on an officer's attested views would mean. [minutes](../markdown/ga49_2022.md)
- **[2008-14 — White v. Siouxlands Presbytery](../cases/ga38_2010__2008-14.md)** (GA38/2010, sustained) — Court erred in refusing a BCO 31-2 investigation into a TE suspected of teaching contrary to the Standards; bears on the existing review-and-control machinery O84 says is inadequate (the "no mechanism to initiate recertification" Whereas). [minutes](../markdown/ga38_2010.md)
- **[2011-06 — Sawyers et al. v. Missouri Presbytery](../cases/ga41_2013__2011-06.md)** (GA41/2013, other) — Court found to have erred in not finding a presumption that a TE held views contrary to the Westminster Standards; illustrates the friction O84 targets, where doctrinal drift surfaces only through contested judicial process rather than routine attestation. [minutes](../markdown/ga41_2013.md)

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
- **31-56 IV** (GA31/2003) — CCB held that neither the Constitution nor the RAO *requires* a presbytery to record a minister's exceptions in its minutes; O84 would impose exactly such an annual recording requirement. [page](../inquiries/ga31_2003__ci02.md)
- **30-29 III (Westminster overture)** (GA30/2002) — An overture mandating that presbyteries record and report all exceptions was found *in conflict* with the Constitution because it would bind a man's conscience beyond what the BCO permits — the core objection any mandatory-attestation scheme must answer. [page](../inquiries/ga30_2002__ci04.md)
- **32-40 II.G** (GA32/2004) — Overture amending the exception-stating requirements (BCO Preface II, ch. 16, 21-4, 24-6.2) found in conflict with the second ordination vow. [page](../inquiries/ga32_2004__ci05.md)
- **33-29 II.D** (GA33/2005) — Mandate requiring officers to explain/account for their doctrinal exceptions found in conflict with BCO Preliminary Principle 1 and WCF 20 (liberty of conscience); bears on compelling officers to articulate disagreement. [page](../inquiries/ga33_2005__ci03.md)
- **38-18 II.1** (GA38/2010) — CCB advised that the BCO provides *no mechanism* for formally recognizing/recording an officer's differences; O84 would create one. [page](../inquiries/ga38_2010__ci01.md)
- **App. O IV.B (42-...)** (GA42/2014) — CCB advised that no constitutional procedure exists to record a candidate's views, and a candidate is not required to list his differences. [page](../inquiries/ga42_2014__ci04.md)
- **51-... II.G** (GA51/2024) — CCB found the overture *adding* to BCO 12-5 (Great Commission requirement) not in conflict, adopted 8-0-0; bears directly because O84 likewise adds a new 12-5 subparagraph. [page](../inquiries/ga51_2024__ci07.md)
- **51-... II.H** (GA51/2024) — CCB found the overture *adding* presbytery-care duties to BCO 13-9 not in conflict, adopted 8-0-0; the structural twin of O84's 13-9.h addition. [page](../inquiries/ga51_2024__ci08.md)

### Prior overtures
- **[GA51 O9](../overtures/ga51_2024__o9.md)** (2024, Answered in the negative) — Add Great Commission requirement to BCO 12-5; the most recent attempt to add a new power-subparagraph to the very provision (12-5) O84 amends — and it failed on the floor. ⭐ [page](../markdown/ga51_2024.md#ga51-p1270)
- **[GA51 O10](../overtures/ga51_2024__o10.md)** (2024, Answered in the negative) — Add Presbytery TE care to BCO 13-9; the companion failed attempt to add to BCO 13-9, the exact provision O84 expands. ⭐ [page](../markdown/ga51_2024.md#ga51-p1270)
- **[GA30 O10](../overtures/ga30_2002__o10.md)** (2002, Adopted/final) — "Specify Good Faith Subscription (Version 2) in BCO"; established the GFS framework and the RAO 16-3 categories O84 expressly builds its attestation on. [page](../markdown/ga30_2002.md#ga30-p75)
- **[GA31 O5](../overtures/ga31_2003__o5.md)** (2003, Adopted/final) — Amend RAO 14-3/14-8 (now RAO 16) regarding confessional subscription; part of the same GFS recording regime O84 invokes via RAO 16-3.e.7. [page](../markdown/ga31_2003.md#ga31-p63)
- **[GA34 O17](../overtures/ga34_2006__o17.md)** (2006, Answered in the negative) — Amend BCO 21-4 ¶7 regarding teaching approved exceptions; a prior attempt to legislate ongoing handling of an officer's stated differences. [page](../markdown/ga34_2006.md#ga34-p207)
- **[GA35 O15](../overtures/ga35_2007__o15.md)** (2007, Answered in the negative) — Amend BCO 21-4 ¶7 regarding teaching of approved exceptions; same theme, again rejected. [page](../markdown/ga35_2007.md#ga35-p166)

### RPR exceptions
None found. The BCO 12 / 13 RPR threads concern review-of-records mechanics (failure to review session minutes, BCO 12-7 / 13-9b; examination of REs, 12-5.b) — not the recording of officers' confessional views. There is no RPR thread on annual attestation of views because no such requirement currently exists, which is the very gap O84 seeks to fill. [by provision](../index/RPR-BY-PROVISION.md)

### Note
Provision-exact spine returned nothing (the join classifies O84 as a non-provision/chapter-level overture: provisions=[]), so all entries above come from a topical search keyed to Good Faith Subscription, recording of officers' views/exceptions, and court-initiated doctrinal review. **Pruning:** the broad "exception/doctrinal" case sweep produced ~64 hits dominated by creation-days subscription disputes (Snapp 1998-01, Mt. Carmel 1997-05) and Revoice/sexuality cases; these are incidental to the *mechanism* O84 creates and were dropped in favor of the three cases that construe a court's affirmative duty to examine an officer's doctrinal accord. **Renumbering:** none — BCO 12 and 13 retain their numbers; older actions cite the same chapter numbers. **Companion cross-link:** GA51 O9/O10 (Metro Atlanta) are the live precedent that adding duty-subparagraphs to 12-5 and 13-9 is constitutionally clean (CCB ci07/ci08) yet politically vulnerable (both Answered in the negative on the floor); the binding-conscience line (CCB 30-29 III, 33-29 II.D) is the most likely ground of objection to the mandatory-attestation feature.

## O85 — Add BCO 44 on Objections
**Targets:** BCO 44 (new chapter, refilling the "Vacated" slot); consequential edits to BCO 45-1, 45-4, 45-5 · **Source:** Northwest Georgia · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-85_NWGA_44.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-85_NWGA_44.pdf)

**What it does:** Moves the "objection" remedy — the right of a court member who lost the right to vote on an appeal/complaint under BCO 39-2 to have a recorded objection — out of BCO 45 ("Dissents, and Protests, and Objections") into a new, dedicated BCO Chapter 44 (currently "Vacated"), striking the objection language from BCO 45-1/45-4 and renumbering 45-5. Stated purpose: objections have a fundamentally different eligibility requirement than dissents/protests, and encouraging them offers a lighter-weight alternative to carrying a complaint/appeal upward, reducing the judicial load on the courts.

**Cites in its own grounds:** BCO 39-2 (loss of vote in appeal/complaint cases); BCO 45; Preliminary Principles 1 and 5; the SJC by way of example. No specific case/overture/inquiry numbers cited.

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
None found. The provision-exact spine returned no cases (provisions=[]). A topical search of CASES.md surfaced only records carrying a "dissent" tag — that tag merely flags that a dissenting opinion is appended; none construe the objection/dissent/protest procedure. Pruned as incidental.

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
- **GA50 II.H (ci08)** (GA50/2023) — CCB found that amending BCO 15-4, 45-1, and 45-4 to let GA commissioners register *objections* to SJC decisions is "not in conflict" with the BCO (Adopted 8-0-0). The most recent constitutional treatment of the very BCO 45-1/45-4 objection language O85 relocates (same matter as GA50 O11 below). ⭐ [page](../inquiries/ga50_2023__ci08.md)
- **20-75 (ci04)** (GA20/1992) — A presbyter may complain against a court's decision to *receive* a protest alleged to be intemperate/disrespectful, since that reception is itself a court action. Construes the BCO 45-5 "temperate language … shall be recorded" clause that O85 carries verbatim into new BCO 44-3. [page](../inquiries/ga20_1992__ci04.md)
- **12-53 II (ci06)** (GA12/1984) — Alleged GA errors may be challenged under BCO 45, and later assemblies cannot annul prior actions. Bears on the function of the BCO 45 dissent/protest/objection remedy O85 reorganizes. [page](../inquiries/ga12_1984__ci06.md)

### Prior overtures
- **[GA50 O11](../overtures/ga50_2023__o11.md)** (2023, Answered in the negative) — "Amend BCO 15-4, 45-1, and 45-4 to Allow GA Commissioner Objections to SJC Decisions" (Platte Valley). The most recent prior attempt to amend the very BCO 45-1/45-4 objection provisions O85 edits; sought to expand who may object, was declined on the floor despite CCB's "not in conflict" advice (II.H above). ⭐ [page](../markdown/ga50_2023.md#ga50-p986), [later p.1084](../markdown/ga50_2023.md#ga50-p1076)
- **[GA29 O17](../overtures/ga29_2001__o17.md)** (2001, Adopted/final) — "Add a New Chapter 44 to BCO and Appendix H" (Central Carolina). Bears on the chapter-44 slot history: O85 relies on BCO 44 being "conveniently vacant," but this overture once populated chapter 44 (cases-without-process / appellate-commission material, appended as Appendix H). [page](../markdown/ga29_2001.md#ga29-p56), [adopt p.141](../markdown/ga29_2001.md#ga29-p141)

### RPR exceptions
- **BCO 39-2** — 3 citations; e.g. [Central Florida](../rpr/exc/central-florida__094.md) 50th (2023) "Protest admitted by a member who did not have a right to vote in a case" (raised), cured at 51st (2024). Real-world friction on exactly the eligibility line O85 codifies — only a member who lost the vote under BCO 39-2 may file an objection. [by provision](../index/RPR-BY-PROVISION.md)
- **BCO 45-5** — 2 citations; [Central Florida](../rpr/central-florida.md) 19th (1991) and [Nashville](../rpr/nashville.md) 36th (2008), both "Protest was not recorded, no explanation given." Friction on the recording duty O85 transplants into new BCO 44-3. [by provision](../index/RPR-BY-PROVISION.md)

### Note
Non-provision overture (creates a new chapter), so the join spine returned provisions=[] — every citation here is from the topical supplement against /workspace/index, with verbatim deep-links. Slot history (not a formal renumbering — no record in bco_renumberings.jsonl): the *original* Chapter 44 was "Voting in Appeals and Complaints," repealed and left vacant at GA11 (1983) — see the minutes motion "Repeal all of Chapter 44 (Voting in Appeals and Complaints) and leave the chapter vacant" [ga11 p.94](../markdown/ga11_1983.md#ga11-p94); GA29 O17 (2001) later reused "Chapter 44" before it was vacated again. O85 simply wants the now-empty slot. Pruning from the first pass: removed a fabricated companion "O86" (no Overture 86 exists in OVERTURES.md) and a mislabeled inquiry "27-43 III" (GA27 27-43 items concern property sale, missionary reception, and SJC vows — none on appeal-vs-complaint); also pruned ~20+ "dissent"-tagged CASES.md records as incidental.

---

## O86 — Amend BCO 43 to Rename Complaints as Inquiries
**Targets:** BCO 43 (and consequential edits to BCO 32-18, 39-1, 39-2, 40-3, 45-1, 45-4) · **Source:** Session of Grace Covenant Church (rejected by Northwest Georgia Presbytery 60th stated mtg.; sent under RAO 11-10) · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-86_GraceCov_43.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-86_GraceCov_43.pdf)

**What it does:** Replaces every occurrence of "complaint" with "inquiry" and "complainant" with "inquirer" throughout BCO 43 (and in the cross-referencing provisions 32-18, 39-1, 39-2, 40-3, 45-1, 45-4), renaming the chapter "Complaints" to "Inquiries." The substance of the procedure is unchanged; the grounds argue the word "complaint" is misconstrued as a formal accusation/charge (BCO 31-32) and is needlessly divisive.

**Cites in its own grounds:** SJC Case 2019-11, Crouse v. Northwest Georgia Presbytery — quoting that "the right to seek redress of improper actions by complaint or appeal is foundational to our Constitutional system" and that mere filing may never alone be grounds to deny membership or office.

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
- **[2019-11 — Crouse v. NW Georgia Presbytery](../cases/ga48_2021__2019-11.md)** (GA48/2021, denied) — Cited verbatim in the overture's grounds; the SJC's affirmation that filing a complaint is a foundational right that may never alone be penalized is the overture's chief warrant for de-stigmatizing the term. [minutes](../markdown/ga48_2021.md#ga48-p804)

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
None found. (See Note — one BCO 43-4 inquiry exists but does not construe the naming question and was pruned.)

### Prior overtures
- **[GA41 O6](../overtures/ga41_2013__o6.md)** (2013, Answered in the negative) — Suncoast Florida sought to amend BCO 43 by adding 43-11 to *define terms in Chapter 43*; the closest prior attempt to fix Chapter 43's terminology, and it was rejected — a direct precedent for how the Assembly has treated definitional tinkering with this chapter. [page](../markdown/ga41_2013.md#ga41-p90)
- **[GA49 O21](../overtures/ga49_2022__o21.md)** (2022, —) — Northwest Georgia sought to amend BCO 43-2 and 43-3 on timing for considering a complaint; recent live amendment activity in this chapter, though substantive (timing) rather than terminological. ⭐ [page](../markdown/ga49_2022.md#ga49-p1326)
- **[GA51 O21](../overtures/ga51_2024__o21.md)** (2025, Approved & ratified) — Central Indiana amended BCO 43-1 to clarify the prohibition on complaints during judicial process; shows the chapter was successfully amended as recently as 2024-25, the baseline text O86 now proposes to re-word. ⭐ [page](../markdown/ga51_2024.md#ga51-p1165)

### RPR exceptions
- **BCO 43-8** — 9 citations (e.g., [Northwest Georgia](../rpr/exc/northwest-georgia__036.md) 49th/2022; [Catawba Valley](../rpr/catawba-valley.md), [Canada West](../rpr/canada-west.md), [Pacific Northwest](../rpr/exc/pacific-northwest__057.md) 50th-51st/2023-24), repeatedly faulting presbyteries for dismissing "timely and orderly complaints" without a hearing — real-world friction over how complaints are received, the very dynamic the overture says casts complainants as adversaries. [by provision](../index/RPR-BY-PROVISION.md)
- **BCO 43-1 / 43-1-p** — 4 citations ([Covenant](../rpr/exc/covenant__001.md) 19th/1991; [Northern Illinois](../rpr/northern-illinois.md) & [South Texas](../rpr/south-texas.md) 30th-31st/2002-03) for failing to record a complaint or improperly ruling it out of order; bears on how the foundational right under 43-1 is administered. [by provision](../index/RPR-BY-PROVISION.md)

### Note
Provision-exact join returned `provisions=[]` (chapter-level overture), so this page is built by topical search of /workspace/index. **Companion GA53 overtures:** O86 also touches BCO 32-18, 39-1/39-2, 40-3, 45-1/45-4 — check for sibling GA53 overtures editing those chapters that may collide with the rename. **No renumbering** of BCO 43 was found (bco_renumberings.jsonl), so older actions cite the same numbers. **Pruned:** (1) Inquiry 12-53 II,56 (GA12/1984, BCO 43-4 — scope of debate prohibitions during a complaint) construes a different question (debate, not the term's meaning) and is incidental to a pure rename; (2) the many substantive BCO 43 procedural overtures in OVERTURES.md (filing-period extensions and hearing/reference amendments at GA14, GA27, GA29, GA40, GA42, etc.) — none addresses the naming/terminology question, so only the definitional precedent (GA41 O6) and the most recent live amendments (GA49, GA51) are retained as bearing.

## O87 — Change the Boundaries of Pittsburgh Presbytery and the Ohio Presbytery
**Targets:** (boundaries) · **Source:** Pittsburgh · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/Overture-87_Pittsburgh_Boundaries-5.15.26.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/Overture-87_Pittsburgh_Boundaries-5.15.26.pdf)

**What it does:** Transfers all Ohio counties currently within Pittsburgh Presbytery's bounds (the region "east and south of and including the counties of Columbiana, Carroll, and Monroe") to Ohio Presbytery, since Ohio Presbytery has since been formed and in 2025 the only PCA church in those Ohio counties of Pittsburgh closed.

**Cites in its own grounds:** None by number — the grounds only quote Pittsburgh's existing official boundary description, note that Ohio Presbytery has since been formed, and recite the 2025 closure of the lone affected PCA church.

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
None found.

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
None found.

### Prior overtures
- **[GA45 O20](../overtures/ga45_2017__o20.md)** (2017, Adopted (final)) — Pittsburgh, "Reassign Ohio Counties from Pittsburgh Presbytery to Ohio Presbytery"; the *direct predecessor* — Pittsburgh did this identical Ohio-county-to-Ohio-Presbytery reassignment once before, and O87 completes the remaining transfer. [page](../markdown/ga45_2017.md#ga45-p674)
- **[GA45 O23](../overtures/ga45_2017__o23.md)** (2017, Adopted (final)) — Ohio, "Concur with Pittsburgh Presbytery to Reassign Counties to Ohio Presbytery"; Ohio's concurring half of that 2017 transfer — exactly the paired-overture structure O87 (Pittsburgh) / O10 (Ohio) now repeats. [page](../markdown/ga45_2017.md#ga45-p678)
- **[GA52 O36](../overtures/ga52_2025__o36.md)** (2025, Adopted (final)) — Georgia Foothills, "Change the Boundaries of Georgia Foothills and Metro Atlanta Presbyteries"; recent two-presbytery transfer modeling the paired-concurrence pattern. ⭐ [page](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p1273)
- **[GA52 O46](../overtures/ga52_2025__o46.md)** (2025, —) — Metro Atlanta, "Change the Boundaries of Georgia Foothills and Metro Atlanta Presbyteries"; the concurring companion from the other affected presbytery — same two-overture structure. ⭐ [page](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p1297)
- **[GA37 O19](../overtures/ga37_2009__o19.md)** (2009, Adopted (final)) — Great Lakes, "Form Ohio Presbytery"; the originating act that created the receiving presbytery and made Pittsburgh's Ohio counties an anomaly this overture removes. [page](../markdown/ga37_2009.md#ga37-p233)
- **[GA37 O21](../overtures/ga37_2009__o21.md)** (2009, Answered by reference) — Ascension, "Concur with Formation of New Ohio Presbytery"; the concurring companion to the Ohio formation. [page](../markdown/ga37_2009.md#ga37-p240)
- **[GA44 O24](../overtures/ga44_2016__o24.md)** (2016, Adopted (final)) — Ohio Presbytery, "Form Columbus Metropolitan Presbytery"; most recent reshaping of Ohio Presbytery's own bounds, showing this territory has been actively redrawn. [page](../markdown/ga44_2016.md#ga44-p259)
- **[GA30 O14](../overtures/ga30_2002__o14.md)** (2002, Answered in the negative) — Rocky Mountain, "Transfer Northern West Virginia Counties to Pittsburgh Presbytery"; prior boundary overture directly touching Pittsburgh's bounds — denied because filed by a non-affected presbytery without the affected presbyteries' concurrence, the negative foil to O87/O10's proper paired filing. [page](../markdown/ga30_2002.md#ga30-p75)

### RPR exceptions
None found.

### Note
**Companion overture:** O87 (Pittsburgh) is the ceding-presbytery half of a paired filing with **O10** (Ohio Presbytery) — see [O10.md](./O10.md); both seek the identical transfer of Pittsburgh's Ohio counties to Ohio Presbytery, satisfying the standard requirement that both affected presbyteries concur. The single most-bearing precedent is **GA45 O20/O23 (2017)**, where these same two presbyteries did this exact Pittsburgh-to-Ohio reassignment with the identical two-overture concurrence structure; O87 finishes the job. This is a non-provision (boundaries) overture, so the deterministic provision-join returned no cases/inquiries/CCB advice/RPR (provisions=[]); every prior action above was found by topical search of OVERTURES.md (and the GA45 O20/O23 predecessor was missed by the looser first pass and the companion O10 file). No judicial case, constitutional inquiry, or RPR exception bears on a routine inter-presbytery boundary transfer.

## O88 — Instruct the AC to Format the BCO for Ease of Printing
**Targets:** (BCO format) — no constitutional provision · **Source:** Siouxlands · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-88_Siouxlands_BCO.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/04/Overture-88_Siouxlands_BCO.pdf)

**What it does:** Directs the Administrative Committee to reformat the BCO, RAO, OMSJC, Certificate of Incorporation, and Corporate Bylaws to a standard 8.5"x11" size, and to make them — along with all future change packets — available as a free digital download (citing the cost, delay, irregular binder-size, and inefficiency of the current printed change packets at $10.80 plus shipping).

**Cites in its own grounds:** None — the whereas clauses cite only practical facts (change-packet cost, production delay, irregular trim size), no prior cases, overtures, or inquiries.

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
None found.

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
None found.

### Prior overtures
- **[GA20 O2](../overtures/ga20_1992__o2.md)** (1992, no recorded outcome) — "Print RAO to Fit in Looseleaf BCO," Missouri Presbytery to AC. The most on-point precedent: a presbytery asking the AC to standardize the physical print format of the RAO so it fits the BCO binder — the same physical-format-and-printing concern O88 raises. [p.58](../markdown/ga20_1992.md#ga20-p56), [p.132](../markdown/ga20_1992.md#ga20-p130)
- **[GA29 O18](../overtures/ga29_2001__o18.md)** (2001, Other) — "Publish Corrected Hardback Edition of the Westminster Standards," Heritage Presbytery to AC. A prior request directing the AC to produce a particular printed/published edition of a constitutional document; bears on how the Assembly handles AC-directed publication-format overtures. [p.58](../markdown/ga29_2001.md#ga29-p56), [p.255](../markdown/ga29_2001.md#ga29-p253)
- **[GA40 O21](../overtures/ga40_2012__o21.md)** (2012, Answered in the negative) — "Amend RAO 12-2 to Move Informational Reports Online," James River Presbytery to CCB/AC. A prior attempt to shift denominational printed material to online/digital distribution — the digital-download half of O88's resolution; the Assembly declined. [p.90](../markdown/ga40_2012.md#ga40-p88), [p.719](../markdown/ga40_2012.md#ga40-p717), [p.797](../markdown/ga40_2012.md#ga40-p795)
- **[GA50 O20](../overtures/ga50_2023__o20.md)** (2023, Answered in the negative) — "Request Administrative Committee to Research Use of Electronic Records for Denominational Purposes," Potomac Presbytery to AC. ⭐ Recent AC-directed digital/electronic-records overture in the same family as O88's free-digital-download prayer; answered in the negative. [p.1023](../markdown/ga50_2023.md#ga50-p1015), [p.1085](../markdown/ga50_2023.md#ga50-p1077)

### RPR exceptions
None found.

### Note
Non-provision overture: the deterministic join returned provisions=[] (an administrative directive to the AC about physical page size and digital distribution, touching no BCO/RAO substantive provision), so it yields zero judicial cases, inquiries, CCB advice, or RPR exceptions — none would bear on a printing/formatting matter, so "None found." reflects that by design, not a search gap. All four prior overtures above come from topical search of /workspace/index/OVERTURES.md for the printing-format and digital-distribution concepts. GA20 O2 is the closest analogue (physical print format of a constitutional document); GA40 O21 and GA50 O20 cover the digital-download prayer and were both answered in the negative — a caution that the Assembly has historically been cool to digitization/format-distribution overtures. Pruned from the topical sweep as incidental: GA14 O13 (publish reasons for BCO changes) and GA6 O21 (reprint theological standards), carried in the looser first pass, are dropped as too general; also pruned GA22 O5 (judicial minutes in printed GA minutes), the byFaith magazine/website funding overtures (GA39–40), and the digital-media study-committee overtures (GA48) — editorial/funding/study questions, not print-format-and-free-digital-access of the constitutional documents. No renumbering caveat applies (no constitutional chapter is targeted), and no companion GA53 overture addresses BCO/RAO publication format.

## O89 — Issue a Declaration of Thanksgiving for the USA on the 250th Anniversary
**Targets:** (statement) — no BCO/RAO amendment; grounds invoke BCO 14-6.k · **Source:** Fellowship Presbytery (to OC) · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/Overture-89_Fellowship_250th.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/Overture-89_Fellowship_250th.pdf)

**What it does:** Asks the 53rd GA to issue a formal "Declaration of Thanksgiving for the United States of America on the Occasion of the 250th Anniversary of the Nation's Founding" on July 4, 2026 — spreading the whereas-statements on the minutes and having the AC publish them electronically through byFaith.

**Cites in its own grounds:** No prior GA cases, overtures, or inquiries. Grounds rest on Scripture (Ps. 136:1; 1 Tim. 2:1-2; Ps. 76:10), WCF 5.7 / 20.2, the 1775 pastoral letter of the Synod of New York and Philadelphia, John Witherspoon's 1776 sermon, the U.S. Constitution's First Amendment, and **BCO 14-6.k** (GA's power "to recommend measures for the promotion of charity, truth and holiness through all the churches under its care").

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
None found. (A declaration/statement is non-justiciable; no SJC/CJB case construes the GA's competence to issue a civil-thanksgiving pronouncement.)

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
None found. (Provision-exact spine is empty. A BCO 14-6 inquiry exists — GA10 CI on a Committee of Commissioners channeling cooperative-agreement business, [page](../inquiries/ga10_1982__ci01.md) — but it construes the committee mechanism, not the substantive 14-6.k power to recommend measures, so it is pruned as non-bearing. The other "14-6.k" hits are to *RAO* 14-6.k, an unrelated nominating rule.)

### Prior overtures
- **[GA3 O20](../overtures/ga03_1975__o20.md)** (1975, Adopted) — "Call for a Day of Prayer and Fasting on July 4, 1976": the PCA's prior Independence-Day / founding-anniversary act (Bicentennial), the closest precedent for a GA observance tied to a U.S. founding milestone. [p.32](../markdown/ga03_1975.md#ga03-p32)
- **[GA19 O41](../overtures/ga19_1991__o41.md)** (1991, Adopted) — "Call a Day of Thanksgiving for War Victory": closest substantive analog — a GA-issued thanksgiving keyed to a national/civil event. [p.61](../markdown/ga19_1991.md#ga19-p59), [p.174](../markdown/ga19_1991.md#ga19-p172)
- **[GA21 O16](../overtures/ga21_1993__o16.md)** (1993, Adopted) — "Issue Declaration of Conscience on Homosexuality to the President": GA exercising the same declarative power (14-6.k genre) to address the civil sphere. [p.56](../markdown/ga21_1993.md#ga21-p54), [p.131](../markdown/ga21_1993.md#ga21-p129)
- **[GA48 O48](../overtures/ga48_2021__o48.md)** (2021, Adopted) — "Repudiate Anti-Asian Racism and Affirm the Dignity of Asian Americans": recent GA-adopted formal statement, illustrating the "spread-on-the-minutes" declaration mechanism O89 follows. ⭐ [p.1116](../markdown/ga48_2021.md#ga48-p1099), [p.1149](../markdown/ga48_2021.md#ga48-p1132)
- **[GA48 O45](../overtures/ga48_2021__o45.md)** (2021, Answered by reference) — "Adopt Statement Seeking Asian American Flourishing in the PCA": recent statement overture answered by reference rather than adopted as its own declaration — shows the OC's frequent disposition of free-standing statement overtures. ⭐ [p.1106](../markdown/ga48_2021.md#ga48-p1089), [p.1149](../markdown/ga48_2021.md#ga48-p1132)
- **[GA49 O26](../overtures/ga49_2022__o26.md)** (2022) — "Adopt a Statement on Political Violence" (also to OC): contemporary statement overture touching the civil/political sphere; corpus records no final disposition, but it bears as a recent instance of the same form. ⭐ [p.1354](../markdown/ga49_2022.md#ga49-p1337), [p.1425](../markdown/ga49_2022.md#ga49-p1408)
- **[GA46 O35](../overtures/ga46_2018__o35.md)** (2018, Adopted) — "Establish Subcommittee of AC to Plan PCA 50th Anniversary Celebration": precedent for the GA formally marking a major anniversary. [p.79](../markdown/ga46_2018.md#ga46-p77), [p.116](../markdown/ga46_2018.md#ga46-p114)

### RPR exceptions
None found. (Presbytery-records exceptions track BCO compliance at the presbytery level; a GA-floor declaration does not generate RPR review.)

### Note
**Companion GA53 triplet:** O89 is one of three materially identical 250th-anniversary thanksgiving-declaration overtures this Assembly — **O66 (Philadelphia)** and **O76 (Calvary)** are the other two — all to OC and all likely to be perfected/merged on the floor. O89 is the most heavily documented (extensive 1775 Synod pastoral-letter and Witherspoon citations).
The provision-exact spine returned nothing (statement overture, `provisions=[]`), so every bearing action here comes from topical search (concepts: thanksgiving, national/founding anniversary, GA-issued declaration/statement, day of prayer). Highest-value precedents: GA3 O20 (prior July-4/founding-anniversary act) and GA19 O41 (prior GA "thanksgiving" keyed to a civil event); GA21 O16 confirms the GA has used the same declarative mechanism toward the civil sphere; recent statement overtures (GA48 O45/O48, GA49 O26 ⭐) show the OC channel and the spread of outcomes (adopted vs. answered by reference). Pruned: 1 incidental BCO 14-6 inquiry (GA10, committee-channeling — not the 14-6.k substantive power). No judicial cases or RPR exceptions bear: a thanksgiving declaration is non-justiciable. No renumbering caveat — BCO 14-6 has carried this numbering.

## O90 — Append Reformed Christian Politics to AIC Report on Christian Nationalism
**Targets:** (committee — no BCO provision) · **Source:** Grace PC (sent under RAO 11-10) · **PDF:** [https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/Overture-90_GracePC_CN.pdf](https://pcaga.org/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/Overture-90_GracePC_CN.pdf)

**What it does:** Asks GA53 to supplement the Ad Interim Committee on Christian Nationalism's Report with a separate "Reformed Christian Politics Study Report" (authored by Stephen Wolfe, TE Zach Garris, TE Sean McGowan) as an appendix, commending that appendix to the churches as pious advice. (Rejected by Palmetto Presbytery May 14, 2026; forwarded by the Session of Grace PC.)

**Cites in its own grounds:** None. The whereas clauses make only generic references to "the Committee on Christian Nationalism's Report" and "our own Reformed tradition of political theology"; no specific prior case, overture, or inquiry is cited.

### Judicial cases (SJC/CJB)
- **[1 — Stephen M. Lee, et al. v. Gulf Coast Presbytery](../cases/ga10_1982__case1.md)** (GA10/1982, complaint sustained in part) — The PCA's leading judicial treatment of whether a particular view of the application of God's law ("theonomy") is within the system of doctrine; directly the kind of political-theology dispute the Christian Nationalism committee is studying and that O90's appendix would address. Bears on substance, not on the procedural mechanism of appending a report. [minutes](../markdown/ga10_1982.md)
- **[2015-13 — Barnes v. Heartland Presbytery](../cases/ga45_2017__2015-13.md)** (GA45/2017, sustained) — Adjudicated stated differences on WCF 19 (the law of God), republication, and "two kingdoms"/Klinean theology as fundamentals of the system of doctrine — the confessional terrain (church/civil-magistrate relation) at the center of the Christian Nationalism study. Bears on the doctrinal subject matter, not on the appendix procedure. [minutes](../markdown/ga45_2017.md)

### Constitutional inquiries / CCB advice
- **11-36 III, 29** (GA11/1983) — CCB advised that a presbytery retains the right to examine and judge a man heretical on WCF 19-4 grounds with specific evidence; bears on how the PCA has handled the orthodoxy of judicial-law / political-theology views that the proposed report engages. [page](../inquiries/ga11_1983__ci01.md)

### Prior overtures
- **[GA52 O3](../overtures/ga52_2025__o3.md)** (2025, answered by reference) — Arizona Presbytery, "Erect Ad Interim Committee on Christian Nationalism"; one of the overtures that created the very committee whose report O90 seeks to supplement. ⭐ [page](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p1167)
- **[GA52 O4](../overtures/ga52_2025__o4.md)** (2025, answered by reference) — South Texas Presbytery, "Erect Ad Interim Study Committee on Christian Nationalism" (naming Moscow theology and postmillennial theonomic reconstructionism); directly defines the committee's mandate that O90 would append to. ⭐ [page](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p1168)
- **[GA52 O47](../overtures/ga52_2025__o47.md)** (2025, adopted/final) — Great Lakes Presbytery, "Erect an Ad Interim Study Committee on Christian Nationalism"; the adopted overture that actually erected the committee. The most directly bearing prior action. ⭐ [page](../markdown/ga52_2025.md#ga52-p1298)
- **[GA24 O9](../overtures/ga24_1996__o9.md)** (1996, answered in the negative) — Southern Florida Presbytery requested a study committee to define and defend or refute "Theonomy"/"Christian Reconstructionism"; a prior, failed attempt at the same political-theology study question now revived by the Christian Nationalism committee and O90's appendix. [page](../markdown/ga24_1996.md#ga24-p52)
- **[GA11 O8](../overtures/ga11_1983__o8.md)** (1983, answered in the negative) — Illiana Presbytery sought to rescind the Seventh GA's statement on judicial law and theonomy; shows the long-running PCA contest over how the courts should treat theonomic political theology. [page](../markdown/ga11_1983.md#ga11-p44)
- **[GA46 O29](../overtures/ga46_2018__o29.md)** (2018, adopted/final) — Pittsburgh Presbytery formed a study committee to examine the RPCNA report on sexual orientation; precedent for the PCA receiving/commending an outside or sister-tradition study report — the mechanism O90 proposes for the Wolfe/Garris/McGowan report. [page](../markdown/ga46_2018.md#ga46-p729)
- **[GA29 O20](../overtures/ga29_2001__o20.md)** (2001, answered in the negative) — New River Presbytery, "Allow Exceptions on Length of Creation Days": the whereas clauses object that the 28th GA's action on the Creation Study Committee was "described by the Moderator as simply 'pious advice'" yet was generating pressure on presbyteries — an exact parallel to the "commend as pious advice" mechanism O90 invokes and the disputes that label generates. [page](../markdown/ga29_2001.md#ga29-p57)

### RPR exceptions
None found. (No BCO provision is targeted, so there is no provision-keyed RPR exception thread.)

### Note
Non-provision (committee) overture: the deterministic spine returned provisions=[], so all bullets above come from topical search of /workspace/index (OVERTURES.md, cases.jsonl, INQUIRIES.md, overture_bodies.jsonl), not from the provision join. No renumbering caveat applies (no BCO target). PRUNED as incidental: Antioch Session v. Eastern Carolina (1992-9a, GA22) — theonomy appears only as one of several topics (creation, divorce, licensure) and does not construe the political-theology question; the homosexuality study-report overture GA47 O39 and the GA48 white-supremacy / CRT study-committee overtures were considered as study-committee precedents but pruned to keep the list to the most on-point pious-advice / append-a-report and Christian-Nationalism actions. Two distinct lines bear here and should be read separately: (1) SUBSTANCE — the theonomy/two-kingdoms/civil-magistrate cases and the GA11/GA24 overtures and CCB advice, which show the PCA's prior handling of the doctrine; and (2) MECHANISM — the GA52 committee-erection overtures (the committee being supplemented) plus the "commend as pious advice" precedent (GA29 O20) and the study-report-reception precedent (GA46 O29). The GA52 O3/O4/O47 trio is the highest-value bearing action. Any companion GA53 overtures concerning the Christian Nationalism committee report should be cross-checked.
